2Corinthians13:10 Looloo tax ma bind leen lii bala maa dikk, ba buma dikkee, du jar may mettil ni may jëflante ak yeen, ci kaw sañ-sañ bi ma Boroom bi jox. Ndax kat sañ-sañ bi, yokke moo ko taxa jóg, waaye deesu ko yàqe." 
2Corinthians13:11 Ma tëje fii nag, bokk yi, bégleen, yokkuleen ba mat sëkk, ñaaxanteleen, mànkooleen te jàmmoo. Su ko defee Yàlla miy Yàllay cofeel ak jàmm mooy ànd ak yeen." 
2Corinthians13:12 Saafoonteeleen fóonante yu sell. Ñu sell ñépp a ngi leen di nuyu. 
2Corinthians13:13 Sunu yiwu Sang Yeesu Almasi nag, ak cofeelu Yàlla, ak bennoo geek Noo gu Sell gi, yal nañu bokk ànd ak yeen ñépp." 
Galatians1:1 Ci man Póol, ndaw li bàyyikoowul ci ay nit, jottliwul yónnentu nit, xanaa Yeesu Almasi, ak Yàlla Baay bi ko dekkal, ci man la kàddu gii bawoo," 
Galatians1:2 bawoo itam ci mboolem bokk yi nekk ak man, ñeel mboolooy gëmkat yu diiwaanu Galasi." 
Galatians1:3 Aw yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen, tukkee ci Yàlla sunu Baay, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi," 
Galatians1:4 mi maye bakkanam ngir njotug sunuy bàkkaar, ba musal nu ci jamonoy tey ju bon ji, ci coobarey Yàlla sunu Baay," 
Galatians1:5 bi daraja ñeel, tey ak ëllëg ba fàww. Amiin." 
Galatians1:6 Man de jaaxle naa ci nii ngeen gaawa dëddoo Yàlla mi leen woo ci boppam, ci ndimbalal yiwu Almasi, bay topp xaat beneen xibaaru jàmmeey!" 
Galatians1:7 Te beneen dafa amul sax, xanaa ñenn ñi leen di jaxase, te bëgga sopparñi xibaaru jàmm bu Almasi." 
Galatians1:8 Waaye nun ci sunu bopp, mbaa malaaka mu bawoo asamaan sax, ku leen ci àgge woon beneen xibaaru jàmm bu dul bi nu leen àgge, kooku yal na alku!" 
Galatians1:9 Wax nanu ko ba noppi, ma waxati ko tey: képp ku leen àgge beneen xibaaru jàmm bu moy bi ngeen xasa jot, yal na alku!" 
Galatians1:10 Léegi nag ndax nit ñi laay sàkkoo jubool, am Yàlla? Am nit ñi laay wuta neex? Su ma bëggoona wéye neex nit ñi de, duma doon jaamub Almasi." 
Galatians1:11 Bokk yi, ma xamal leen ne leen xibaaru jàmm bi may yégle, bàyyikoowul ci nit." 
Galatians1:12 Te it man jëlewuma ko, jàngewuma ko ci nit, xanaa ci peeñum Yeesu Almasi." 
Galatians1:13 Ndax kat dégg ngeen ni ma doon jëfe bu jëkk, bi ma nekkee ci yoonu Yawut, bundxatal gu jéggi dayo ga ma daan teg mbooloom gëmkati Yàlla mi, di ko yàq." 
Galatians1:14 Yoonu Yawut, maa ci rawoon ñu bare ci sama maas gi ma bokkal askan, te maa leen gënoona xér fuuf ci sunu aaday maam." 
Galatians1:15 Waaye ca sama biiru ndey la ma Yàlla séddoo, woo ma ci boppam ci kaw yiwam, te moom la soob," 
Galatians1:16 mu feeñalal ma Doomam, ba ma àgge jaambur ñi dul Yawut, xibaaru jàmm bi ci mbirum Almasi. Ci saa si diisoowuma ci ak kenn." 
Galatians1:17 Demuma sax Yerusalem, seeti ñi ma jëkka doon ndawi Almasi, waaye Arabi laa dem, doora délsi Damaas." 
Galatians1:18 Gannaaw ba ñu ca tegee ñetti at laa doora dem Yerusalem, ngir xamanteji ak Sefas, toog fa moom ñaari ayi bés." 
Galatians1:19 Teewul gisuma kenn ci ndaw yi ci des, ku dul Yanqóoba, rakku Sang bi." 
Galatians1:20 Li ma leen bind nii nag, Yàlla mi nu tiim seere na ne du ay fen." 
Galatians1:21 Gannaaw gi laa dem diiwaani Siri ak Silisi. 
Galatians1:22 Waaye ba boobu, mboolooy gëmkati Almasi ya ca diiwaanu Yude xamuñu ma woon." 
Galatians1:23 Déggoon nañu rekk ñu naan: «Ki nu daan bundxatal bu jëkk, di yàq sunu yoonu ngëm wi de, léegi mooy yégle xibaaru jàmm bi koy xamle!»" 
Galatians1:24 Mboolooy gëmkat yooyu nag di sant Yàlla ci man. 
Galatians2:1 Fukki at ak ñeent gannaaw gi laa dellu Yerusalem, ànd ak Barnaba, yóbbaale Tit itam." 
Galatians2:2 Sama tànk yooyu nag am peeñu moo ko waral. Ca laa wéetoo ak ña ñu jàppoon ne ñooy kàngami mbooloom gëmkat ña, faramfàcceel leen xibaaru jàmm bi may yégal jaambur ñi dul Yawut, ngir ragal sama liggéey bi ma jota def, te di ko wéye, doon coonob neen." 
Galatians2:3 Moonte Tit mi ma àndaloon sax, tegeesu ko fa wartéefu xaraf, te ci askanu gereg yi dul xaraf la bokk." 
Galatians2:4 Doonte booba, ay nit ñu tuddoo bokki gëmkat ñoo yoxoosu ba tàbbi ci sunu biir, di nu yëddu, ngir luqatu ni nu moome sunu bopp ndax Almasi Yeesu mi nu gëm, te li ñu ci jublu di delloo nu ci buumi njaam." 
Galatians2:5 Waaye ñooñu, nangulunu leen lu tollook simili sax, ndax bëgg leena sàmmal yeen, dëggug xibaaru jàmm bi, ba mu sax ci yeen." 
Galatians2:6 Teewul ñooñu ñu jàppe woon ay kàngam, ak daraja ju ñu masoona am, amalu ma solo, nde Yàlla amul xejj ak seen, ñooñu yokkuñu lenn ci kàddu gi may xamle." 
Galatians2:7 Xanaa kay li ñu gis moo di ni Yàlla yebale Piyeer ngir mu àgge askanu Yawut xibaaru jàmm bi, noonu la ma yebale ngir ma àgge ko jaambur ñi xaraful," 
Galatians2:8 ndax ki liggéey ci Piyeer, ngir mu doon ndawam ci Yawut yi, moo liggéey ci man itam, ngir may ndawam ci yeneen xeet yi." 
Galatians2:9 Ña ñu jàppoon ne ñooy kenuy mbooloom gëmkat ña nag, te ñuy Yanqóoba ak Sefas ak Yowaan, ba ñu ràññee yiw wi ñu ma jagleel, maak Barnaba lañu jox loxo, ngir nun nu liggéeyi ca jaambur ña, te ñoom ñu liggéeyi ci Yawut yi." 
Galatians2:10 Laajuñu lu moy nu fàttliku néew doole yi, te loolu di lu ma pastéefoo jëfe." 
Galatians2:11 Waaye ba Sefas dikkee Àncos, jàkk laa ko def, weddi ko, ndax moo nekkul woon ci dëgg." 
Galatians2:12 Ndax kat balaa aw nit a dikk, bàyyikoo fa Yanqóoba, Sefas da daan bokk lekk ak jaambur ñi dul Yawut. Waaye ba ñooñu dikkee la rocciku, daldi beddeeku jaambur ñi, ndax ragal waa làng, ga jàpp ne aaday xaraf wartéef la." 
Galatians2:13 Yeneen Yawut ya it di jinigalandoo, ba Barnaba sax lajj topp leen ci seenug jinigal." 
Galatians2:14 Waaye ba ma gisee ne doxewuñu njub gi dëggug xibaaru jàmm bi laaj, maa wax Sefas ci kanam ñépp, ne ko: «Ndegam yaw miy ab Yawut, yaa jëfewul ni ab Yawut, xanaa di jëfe ni xeeti jaambur ñi, ana lu tax ngay ërtal jaambur ñi dul ay Yawut, ngir ñu yawutal?»" 
Galatians2:15 Nun danoo juddu diy Yawut, te bokkunu ca xeet yee diy bàkkaarkat." 
Galatians2:16 Xam nanu nag ne nit ki, du ci jëfi sàmm ndigali yoon la ko Yàlla di joxe àtteb ku jub, xanaa ci ngëm gu mu gëm Yeesu Almasi. Te nun itam, Almasi Yeesu lanu gëm, ngir Yàlla jox nu àtteb ku jub ci kaw gëm gu nu gëm Almasi, te du ci kaw jëf ju nu sàmme ndigali yoon. Ndax kat du ci jëfi sàmm yoon lees di joxe kenn àtteb ku jub." 
Galatians2:17 Ba tey su nu dee sàkku àtteb ku jub, ndax li nu gëm Almasi, te teewul nit ñi gis ne nu ngi bàkkaar, nun itam, ndax loolu day wund ne Almasi mooy xiirtale ci bàkkaar? Mukk kay!" 
Galatians2:18 Ndaxam su dee tabaxub ndigalu yoon bi ma tojoon, moom laa tabaxaat, maa def sama bopp moykatub yoon." 
Galatians2:19 Su dee wàllu yoonu Musaa nag, man nit ku dee laa, te yoonu Musaa moo ko waral, ngir ma mana dund dund gu ñeel Yàlla. Dees maa boole ak Almasi rey ca bant ba." 
Galatians2:20 Moo tax dootu man maay dund, waaye Almasi mooy dund léegi ci man. Sama dundu yaramu suux wii tey nag, ci ngëm gi ma gëm Doomu Yàlla laa koy dunde, moom mi ma sopp, ba jébbale boppam ngir man." 
Galatians2:21 Duma neenal yiwu Yàlla, ndax kat su doon ci sàmm ndigalu yoon lees di ame àtteb ku jub, konoon Almasi moo dee cig neen." 
Galatians3:1 Yeen waa Galasi, yeena ñàkk xel! Ku leen gëlëmal, te na Yeesu Almasi deeye ca bant ba di lu ñu leen leeralal ba mu mel ni lu ngeen gise seeni bët?" 
Galatians3:2 Lenn rekk laa bëgg ngeen xamal ma ko: ndax ci jëfi sàmm ndigalu yoon ngeen jote Noowug Yàlla gi, am li ngeen dégg xibaaru jàmm bi ba gëm ko moo leen ko may?" 
Galatians3:3 Ana nu ngeen mana ñàkke nii xel? Ngeen tàmbalee ci Noo gi, ba noppi di jéema mottlikoo jëfi nitu suuxu neen!" 
Galatians3:4 Dangeena dékku yii coono yépp ci neen? Xanaa déet kay! 
Galatians3:5 Ki leen di may Noo gi, tey sottal ay kéemaan ci seen biir, ndax li ngeen sàmm yoon moo tax mu di ko def, am li ngeen dégg, ba gëm moo tax?" 
Galatians3:6 Noonu la Ibraayma gëme Yàlla, «ñu waññal ko ngëmam ag njub.»" 
Galatians3:7 Xamleen boog ne nit ñiy boroom ngëm, ñooñu ñooy doomi Ibraayma." 
Galatians3:8 Mbind mi moo waajaloon lu jiitu ne ci kaw ngëm lees di joxe xeet yi dul Yawut, àtteb nit ñu jub. Moo taxoon mu yégal Ibraayma lu jiitu, bii xibaaru jàmm: «Xeeti àddina yépp ci yaw lañuy barkeele,»" 
Galatians3:9 ba tax na, boroom ngëm yi lees di booleek Ibraayma miy boroom ngëm, barkeel leen." 
Galatians3:10 Mboolem ñi yaakaar seen jëf ju ñu sàmme yoonu Musaa, repp nañoo alku, nde bindees na ne: «Alkànde ñeel na képp ku saxoowul mboolem digal yi ñu bind ci téereb yoon wi, ngir di ko jëfe.»" 
Galatians3:11 Li sàmm yoon taxul kenn jot àtteb ku jub fi kanam Yàlla sax, lu leer nàññ la, nde: «Ku jub ndax ngëmam mooy dund.»" 
Galatians3:12 Yoon wi nag ajuwul ci ngëm, nde: «Kuy jëfe digal yooyu, yaay dund ndax ñoom.»" 
Galatians3:13 Almasi moom, moo nu jot ci alkàndey yoon wi, ba mu doonee ku alku ngir nun, nde: «Alkute ñeel na képp ku ñu rey, wékk ko ci bant.»" 
Galatians3:14 Noonu la deme ngir barkeb Ibraayma wàccal xeet yi dul Yawut ndax Almasi Yeesu, ngir itam nu jot ci digeb Noo gu Sell gi, ci kaw ngëm." 
Galatians3:15 Bokk yi, ma misaale ko mbiri doom Aadama. Kayitub donale bu nit doŋŋ bind, su dee lu wóor, deesu ko neenal, mbaa di ci yokk dara." 
Galatians3:16 Te Ibraayma lañu digoon dige yi mook ki taxawal askanam. Newuñu: «ñi taxawal ay askanam», mbete ñu bare lañuy wax, waaye wenn rekk la: «ki taxawal askanam,» te ki taxawal askanam moo di Almasi." 
Galatians3:17 Li ma ciy wax mooy lii: kóllëreg Yàlla gi taxawe ni kayitu donale gu mu dëggal, yoonu Musaa, wi dikk ñeenti téeméeri at ak fanweer gannaaw kóllëre gi, manu koo neenal, ba fomm digeb Yàlla." 
Galatians3:18 Su doon ci yoonu Musaa la ndonale ga aju, kon dootul doon lu digeb Yàlla waral. Waaye ci kaw ab dige la Yàlla baaxee Ibraayma aw yiwam." 
Galatians3:19 Waaw kon yoonu Musaa, ana luy njariñam? Dees koo toftal ca dige ba, ngir muy fésal moyi nit ñi ba keroog boroom dige, bi taxawal askanu Ibraayma, dikk. Ay malaaka ñoo biral yoon wi, ci ndimbalal ab jottlikat." 
Galatians3:20 Ab jottlikat nag ñaar a koy séq, te Yàlla kenn doŋŋ la." 
Galatians3:21 Ndax kon yoonu Musaa dafa juuyoo ak digey Yàlla? Mukk kay. Ndax kat su fekkoon ne dañoo maye wenn yoon wu mana may nit ku ko sàmm, mu dund, konoon àtteb ku jub fi kanam Yàlla mana jóge dëgg ci sàmm gu nit ki sàmm yoon wi." 
Galatians3:22 Waaye mbind mi biral na ne mboolem àddina moo tënku ci kilifteefu bàkkaar, ngir dige bi gëm Yeesu Almasi di jagle, mana dikkal aji gëm ñi." 
Galatians3:23 Balaa yoonu ngëm wee dikk, dees noo jàppoon tënk ci yoonu Musaa, ba kera yoonu ngëm wi feeñee." 
Galatians3:24 Noonu la yoonu Musaa doone sunu njaatige, tette nu ba ci Almasi, ngir nu jagoo àtteb nit ñu jub ci kaw ngëm." 
Galatians3:25 Waaye léegi, bi yoonu ngëm wi dikkee, nekkatunu ci kilifteefu njaatige." 
Galatians3:26 Yeen ñépp doomi Yàlla ngeen, ndax li ngeen gëm Almasi Yeesu." 
Galatians3:27 Ndax kat mboolem yeen ñi ñu sóob sóobeb Almasi, jëmmu Almasi ngeen soloo." 
Galatians3:28 Kon nag amul Yawut ak ku dul Yawut, amul ab jaam ak as gor, amul góor ak jigéen. Yeen ñépp benn ngeen ci Almasi Yeesu." 
Galatians3:29 Te su ngeen bokkee ci Almasi, yeen ay askanu Ibraayma, te yeena jagoo dige ba." 
Galatians4:1 Li ma leen di wax nag mooy lii: boroom ndono li ci kër gi, li feek mu dib tuut-tànk, wuutewul akub jaam, doonte moo moom lépp." 
Galatians4:2 Ci kilifteefu ay wattukat aki saytukat lay nekk ba kera mu àggee ca at ya ko baayam àppaloon. 
Galatians4:3 Nun itam naka noonu, ba nu dee ay tuut-tànk yu nekk ci kilifteefu mbiri àddina, ay jaam lanu woon." 
Galatians4:4 Waaye ba àpp ba jotee, Yàlla moo yónni Doomam, mu juddoo ci jigéen, juddoo ci biir curgag yoonu Musaa," 
Galatians4:5 ngir jot ñi ci curgag yoon wi, ba nu jagoo cérub doom." 
Galatians4:6 Li ngeen diy doom nag tax na Yàlla yebal Noowug Doomam ci seen biir xol, ba Noo gi naan: «Abba», mu firi Baay." 
Galatians4:7 Moo tax dootuloo ab jaam, doom nga. Gannaaw doom nga nag, boroom cér nga it fa Yàlla sa baay." 
Galatians4:8 Bu jëkk, ba ngeen xamul Yàlla, ay yàlla yu dul dëgg ngeen daan jaamu." 
Galatians4:9 Waaye léegi bi ngeen xamee Yàlla, mbaa bi leen Yàlla ràññee, nu ngeen mana delluwaate ci mbiri àddina yooyu boole tële ak ñàkk njariñ, bay nekkaat seeni jaam?" 
Galatians4:10 Yeena ngi wormaal yenn bés yi, aki weer, ak ay fan, aki at!" 
Galatians4:11 Li may ragal ci yeen daal mooy sama coono ci yeen neen. 
Galatians4:12 Yeen laay tinu, bokk yi, mel-leen ni man, ci yooyu mbir, ndax man itam ni yeen laa mel. Tooñuleen ma benn yoon." 
Galatians4:13 Xam ngeen ne tëleg yaram moo ma mayoon yoon wa ma leen jëkka àgge xibaaru jàmm bi. 
Galatians4:14 Nattu ba leen sama woppi yaram tegoon it taxul ngeen jéppi ma, taxul ngeen beddi ma. Ni malaakam Yàlla ngeen ma dalale, mbaa ni Yeesu Almasi" 
Galatians4:15 Ana seen mbég mooma woon nag? Ndax kat maa leen seedeel ne su manoona am sax, seeni bët ngeen di luqi, jox ma." 
Galatians4:16 Xanaa li ma leen di wax dëgg daa tax ma mujj di seenub noon? 
Galatians4:17 Yitte ju réy ji ñenn ñiy taqoo ak yeen de, jubluwuñu ci lu baax. Dañu leena bëgga tàggale ak nun, ba ngeen taq leen." 
Galatians4:18 Yitte ju réy ju ñu am ci nit ki nag, ndegam lu baax lees ci jublu, saa su nekk lay baax, waaye du rekk saa yu ma teewee ci seen biir." 
Galatians4:19 Yeen samay doom! Maa ngi dellooti ci mat wu ma leen jure woon ni jigéen, ba keroog Almasi mate sëkk ci yeen." 
Galatians4:20 Maaka bëggoona nekk ak yeen tey, ba gëna misaale sama baat, nde jàq naa lool ci yeen!" 
Galatians4:21 Waxleen ma, yeen ñi bëgga nekk ci kilifteefu yoonu Musaa, xanaa xamuleen li yoon wi wax?" 
Galatians4:22 Bindees na ne Ibraayma ñaari doom yu góor la am; kenn ki jaam bi jur, ak ki gor si jur." 
Galatians4:23 Doomu jaam bi moo juddu ci kaw coobarey bakkanu nit, waaye ki gor si jur, ci kaw digeb Yàlla la juddu." 
Galatians4:24 Mbir mi misaal a ngi ci. Ñaari jigéen ñi ñaari kóllëre lay bijji. Genn kóllëre gi bawoo tundu Sinayi moo meññ lu ñeel njaam, te kooku mooy Ajara." 
Galatians4:25 Ajara moomu mooy tundu Sinayi, wa ca réewum Arabi, te moo taxawe Yerusalem gii tey, dëkk bii dib jaam mook doomam yi ko dëkke." 
Galatians4:26 Waaye Yerusalem, ga fa kaw, mooy gor si, te moom mooy sunu ndey." 
Galatians4:27 Ndax kat bindees na ne: «Yaw mi jaasir, ba juroo, xaacul, yaw mi xamul mititu mat, sarxolleel, nde ndaw si ñu foñ moo gëna jaboot kiy séy.»" 
Galatians4:28 Yeen nag bokk yi, yeenay doomi digeb Yàlla, ni ko Isaaxa doone." 
Galatians4:29 Waaye doom ji juddoo ci coobarey bakkan, noonu mu daan bundxatale, bu jëkkoon, doom ji juddoo ci Noowug Yàlla, noonu rekk lay deme ba tey jii." 
Galatians4:30 Te lu ci Mbind mi wax? Mu ne: «Dàqal jaam bu jigéen bii ak doomam, ndax doomu jaam bi du donnandoo ak doomu gor si.»" 
Galatians4:31 Kon nag bokk yi, nun dunu doomi jaam bi, waaye nooy doomi gor si." 
Galatians5:1 Almasi da noo yiwi, ngir nu yiwiku, kon nag saxooleen ko, te baña laxasooti buumi njaam." 
Galatians5:2 Dama ne, man Póol maa leen wax ne leen: su ngeen demee ba ñu xarfal leen kay, Almasi amalatu leen lenn njariñ." 
Galatians5:3 Ma artooti képp ku dem ba ñu xarfal ko, ne ko mboolem yoon wi la wara jëfe." 
Galatians5:4 Yeen ñiy sàmm yoonu Musaa, di ko sàkkoo àtteb njub fa kanam Yàlla, daggoo ngeen ak Almasi, ñàkk ngeen yiwu Yàlla." 
Galatians5:5 Ndax nun kat, ci ndimbalal Noo gi, ak ci sunu kaw ngëm lanu yaakaare ñu jox nu àtteb njub bi nuy séentu." 
Galatians5:6 Ci Almasi Yeesu mi nu gëm, xaraf ak ñàkka xaraf, dara amu ci solo; li am solo mooy ngëm, gi jëfi cofeel di firndeel." 
Galatians5:7 Seen njàlbéenu xél de baax na! Ana ku leen gàllankoor ba toppuleen dëgg gi? 
Galatians5:8 Loolu leen fàbbi de jógewul ci ki leen woo. 
Galatians5:9 As lawiir, tooyalub sunguf bépp lay funkil." 
Galatians5:10 Man de gëm naa ndax Boroom bi, ne dungeen wuuteek man xalaat benn yoon ci lii. Waaye kiy jaxase seenum xel, ak ku mu mana doon, mooy gàddu mbugalam." 
Galatians5:11 Man nag bokk yi, su ma dee xiirtale ci xaraf, ana lees may bundxataleeti? Konoon kay sama waareb deewu Almasi ca bant ba dootu doon ag tooñ ci kenn." 
Galatians5:12 Ñi leen di lëjal ak waxi xaraf, nañu xuuf boog seen ngóorag bopp benn yoon!" 
Galatians5:13 Yeen de bokk yi, cig yiwiku lees leen woo. Moytuleen lenn rekk: bu seenug yiwiku diw lay, ngir topp seen bakkan, waaye deeleen surgawoonte ngir cofeel." 
Galatians5:14 Ndax yoonu Musaa wépp, ci lenn ndigal lii la tënku: «Ni ngeen soppe seen bopp, nangeen ko soppe seen moroom.»" 
Galatians5:15 Waaye su ngeen dee màttante ak a lekkante kat, moytuleena far yàqante yaxeet!" 
Galatians5:16 Li ma leen di wax moo di: doxeleen Noowug Yàlla, su boobaa dungeen topp seen xemmemtéefi bakkan." 
Galatians5:17 Ndax bakkan, la muy xemmem, daa dëngoo ak Noo gi; Noo gi it, la muy xemmem dëngoo ak bakkan. Dañu di yaar yu féewaloo, te moo tax dungeen def la ngeen nammoona def." 
Galatians5:18 Waaye su leen Noo gi jiitee, su boobaa nekkatuleen ci kilifteefu yoon wi." 
Galatians5:19 Jëfi bakkan nag yomb naa xàmmi, te mooy: powum séy, ak jëfi sobe, ak yàqute," 
Galatians5:20 ak bokkaale, ak xërëm, ak mbañeel, ak féewaloo, ak kiñaan, ak mer mu ëpp, ak jiital say bëgg-bëgg, ak réeroo, ak xàjjalikoo," 
Galatians5:21 ak ñeetaane, ak màndite, ak mbumbaay, ak yeneen yu ni mel. Ma àrtu leen nag na ma leen artoo woon, ñiy jëfe noonu, amuñu cér ci nguurug Yàlla." 
Galatians5:22 Meññeefum Noowug Yàlla nag moo di: cofeel, ak mbég, ak jàmm, ak xolu muñ, ak mbaax, akug tabe, ak ngëm," 
Galatians5:23 akug teey, ak moom sa bakkan. Yu mel noonu, wenn yoon bañu ko." 
Galatians5:24 Ñi bokk ci Almasi Yeesu nag, ñoo daaj ca bantam ba, seen bakkan, daajaale ko ak sàkkuteefam yu tar, aki xemmemtéefam." 
Galatians5:25 Gannaaw nag Noowug Yàlla moo nu dundal, nanu topp Noo gi." 
Galatians5:26 Bunu di yég sunu bopp, di merloonte ak a iñaanante." 
Galatians6:1 Bokki gëmkat ñi, su ñu bettee nit ci ag tooñ, yeen ñi topp Noowug Yàlla, waññileen ko ndànk, te kenn ku nekk ci yeen xoolaat boppam bu baax, ngir seen bakkan bañ leena xiirtal, ba ngeen daanu ci fiir gu ni mel." 
Galatians6:2 Yennikoonteleen seeni yen, su boobaa ngeen di topp yoonu Almasi ba mu mat sëkk." 
Galatians6:3 Ku foog ne moo am solo, te du dara nag, boppam lay nax." 
Galatians6:4 Ku ci nekk, jëfi boppam, na ko niir. Su ci amee lenn lu mu mana sagoo, na ko yemale ci boppam, te baña sagoo lenni boppam lu mu xool ci ñeneen," 
Galatians6:5 nde ku nekk ak sa añu jëfi bopp. 
Galatians6:6 Ki ñuy jàngal kàddug Yàlla nag war naa sédd ki koy jàngal ci mboolem alalam. 
Galatians6:7 Bu leen lenn nax; Yàlla deesu ko foontoo. Nit ki, li mu ji, moom lay góob." 
Galatians6:8 Ku jiyal bànneexu bakkanam, ci bànneexu bakkanam lay jële ngóobum yàqute; ku jiyal Noowug Yàlla, ci Noo gi ngay góobe texe gu sax dàkk." 
Galatians6:9 Bunu tàyyi ci def lu baax, nde bu jotee rekk nooy góob, ndegam yoqiwunu." 
Galatians6:10 Kon nag bi nu koy jekku, nanuy def lu baax, ngir ñépp, rawatina waa kër yoonu ngëm wi." 
Galatians6:11 Seetluleen mbind mi; ci araf yu mag yii ngeen wara xàmmee, ne sama loxol bopp laa ko binde!" 
Galatians6:12 Ñi leen di gétën ci xaraf mooy ñi ngistal tax ñu bëgg nit ñi gërëme leen seen melow yaram, te jubluwuñu ci lu moy ragal ku leen bundxatal ndax deewug Almasi gi ñuy xamle ne mooy taxa mucc." 
Galatians6:13 Ñi xaraf ñoom ci seen bopp sax toppuñu yoon wi. Teewul ñu bëgg ngeen xaraf, ngir mana damoo seen màndargam yaram, yeen ñi ñu xarafloo." 
Galatians6:14 Waaye man de Yàlla buma damoo lenn lu moy deewug sunu Boroom Yeesu Almasi ca bant ba. Bant boobu moo tax àddina di lu ñu ma daajal ci bant, ba àddina dee; man it may lu ñu daajal àddina ci bant ba ma dee." 
Galatians6:15 Xaraf ak ñàkka xaraf, dara amu ci solo. Li am solo mooy doon mbindeef mu bees." 
Galatians6:16 Mboolem ñiy sàmm ndigal lii nag, te di Israyilu Yàlla, jàmm ak yërmande ñeel na leen." 
Galatians6:17 Li ci des moo di gannaaw-si-tey, bu ma kenn lëjalati, ndax légét yi ci sama yaram, samag bokk ci Yeesu la màndargaal." 
Galatians6:18 Bokk yi, yal na sunu yiwu Boroom Yeesu Almasi ànd ak seenum xel. Amiin." 
Ephesians1:1 Ci man Póol, ndawal Almasi Yeesu ci coobarey Yàlla, ci man la kàddu gii bawoo, ñeel ñu sell ña ca Efes te di ñu sàmm seen kóllëre ak Almasi Yeesu." 
Ephesians1:2 Aw yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen, bawoo fa Yàlla sunu Baay, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
Ephesians1:3 Cant ñeel na Yàlla sunu Baayu Sang Yeesu Almasi, mi nu baaxe bépp barkey biir, ci Almasi mi nu bokk, fa déndi asamaan ya." 
Ephesians1:4 Te mooy noonu mu nu taamoo ba àddina sosoogul ndax Almasi mi nu bokk, ngir nu doon ñu sell te mucc sikk fa kanamam. Ci biir cofeel" 
Ephesians1:5 la dogaloon lu jiitu, ne ci Yeesu Almasi la nuy defe ay doomi boppam, te muy bànneexam, di coobareem." 
Ephesians1:6 Moo tax cant ñeel ko, ndax yiwam wu màgg wi mu nu baawaanal ci Soppeem bi." 
Ephesians1:7 Ci moom lanu ame njot gi nu sottalal njéggalug moy, ndax deretam ji tuuru, noonu ko Yàlla defe ci yiwam wu yaa," 
Ephesians1:8 wi mu nu baawaanal, mayaale nu mépp xel mu rafet akug dégg." 
Ephesians1:9 Moo nu xamal mbóotum coobareem, mi mu nammoona sottale naka jekk ci Almasi, na mu ko neexe." 
Ephesians1:10 Li Yàlla namm, bu fan yi matee, moo di dajale lépp ci kilifteefu Almasi, mboolem la fa asamaan, ak li fi suuf." 
Ephesians1:11 Ci moom lanu jote sunu muur ci kaw dogalu Yàlla mi nu taamu lu jiitu, moom miy sottal lépp ni mu ko namme ci coobareem." 
Ephesians1:12 Moo tax nu di ko sante màggaayam, nun ñi jëkka wékk sunu yaakaar ci Almasi." 
Ephesians1:13 Kooku, yeen ñi dul Yawut, ba ngeen déggee, yeen itam kàddug dëgg gi, xibaaru jàmm, bi jëm ci seenug mucc, gannaaw ba ngeen gëmee, ci moom itam lañu leen màndargaale Noo gu Sell gi ñu dige woon." 
Ephesians1:14 Noo gi moo di dawal bi nu jotagum ci sunu muur, ba kera njotug ñoñi Yàlla matee, ba nit ñi sante Yàlla màggaayam." 
Ephesians1:15 Moo tax man it, bi ma déggee ba tey, seen ngëm ci Sang Yeesu, ak seen cofeel ci ñu sell ñépp," 
Ephesians1:16 noppiwumaa sant Yàlla ndax yeen, te maa ngi leen di fàttliku ci samay ñaan," 
Ephesians1:17 ngir Yàllay sunu Sang Yeesu Almasi, Baay bu màgg bi, sol leen xel mu rafet, ak ngis, ngir ngeen man koo xam bu baax." 
Ephesians1:18 Ngir itam seen bëti xol leer ba ngeen gis yaakaar ji ci wooteem, ak ni ay ngëneelam géejoo te yéeme, ñeel ñu sell ñi mu séddoo." 
Ephesians1:19 Ngeen boole ci xam manooreem gu nattuwul gi mu nu lañalal, nun gëmkat ñi. Manoore googu feeñ na ci jëf ji sottee ci kàttanam ak dooleem," 
Ephesians1:20 ji mu fésal ci Almasi, ba mu ko dekkalee, dëël ko ci ndijooram, fa déndi asamaan." 
Ephesians1:21 Foofa la Almasi tiime lu sore gépp nguur, ak bépp sañ-sañ, ak gépp manoore, ak gépp kilifteef, ak wépp tur wees di tudd, muy tey, di ëllëg." 
Ephesians1:22 Yàlla moo teg lépp fi suufu ndëgguy tànkam, te moo ko def muy bopp bi tiim lépp, ñeel mbooloom gëmkat ñi," 
Ephesians1:23 mbooloo miy aw yaramam. Ci mbooloo mi nag la Almasi teewe teewaay bu mat sëkk, te Almasi mooy matal lépp ci ñépp." 
Ephesians2:1 Yeen dangeena dee woon ndax seeni moy ak seeni bàkkaar," 
Ephesians2:2 yi ngeen doon dunde démb, ngeen àndoon ci ak doxalinu àddinay tey jii, ak ku bon kiy kàngamu boroom baat yi ci jaww, ji asamaan tiim, boroom noo gi wéye liggéeyam ci biir aji déggadi ñi, tey." 
Ephesians2:3 Ci ñoom lanu bokkoon nun ñépp itam; mas nanoo topp sunu bakkan, di jëfe lu sunu bakkan, ak sunum xel xemmem. Sunu bindu nit taxoon na noo yeyoo am sànj ni ñépp." 
Ephesians2:4 Waaye Yàlla mi bare yërmande, ci kaw cofeel gu réy, gi mu nu sopp," 
Ephesians2:5 nun ñi doon nit ñu dee ba noppi ndax sunuy moy, moo nu booleek Almasi, dundalaat nu. Ci kaw yiw daal ngeen mucce." 
Ephesians2:6 Ci sunu bokk ak Yeesu Almasi la nu Yàlla dekkalandoo ak moom, dëëlandoo nook moom fa déndi asamaan." 
Ephesians2:7 Mbaax gi nu Yàlla won ci Almasi Yeesu, moom lay firndeele mboolem xarnu yiy ñëw, ni yiwam yaatoo ba tiiñ am xel." 
Ephesians2:8 Ndax kat ci yiw ngeen mucce ci kaw ngëm, te loolu jógewul ci yeen, mayu Yàlla la;" 
Ephesians2:9 du peyu jëf, ba kenn di ci kañu." 
Ephesians2:10 Ndax kat noo di liggéeyu Yàlla; Yàllaa nu yeesal ci Almasi Yeesu, ngir nu wéye jëf ju rafet, ja mu nu fàgguloon ca njàlbéen, ngir nu di ko jëfe." 
Ephesians2:11 Kon nag, yeen jaambur ñi dul Yawut cib juddu, yeen ñi ñuy wooye yéefar yi xaraful, te ñi leen ko dàkkantale woon di Yawut yi xarafe ci loxol nit ku leen xarfal ci seen yaram, fàttlikuleen seen démb." 
Ephesians2:12 Jant yooyu amuleen woon benn cér ci Almasi, te amuleen woon jenn yelleef ci mbootaayu bànni Israyil. Bokkuleen woon ci kóllëre yi ëmb digeb Yàlla, te mu fasoo ko ak ñoom. Ñàkk yaakaar, ak ñàkka xam Yàlla ngeen nekke woon ci àddina." 
Ephesians2:13 Waaye yeen ñi sore woon, léegi bi ngeen nekkee ci Almasi Yeesu, jege ngeen ndax deretu Almasi ji tuuru." 
Ephesians2:14 Ndaxte moom mooy sunu jàmm, moom mi boole ñaar, Yawut bi ak jaambur bi dul Yawut, def leen kenn. Ci suuxu yaramam wa ñu daaj la ñàggee ñagu mbañeel bi doxoon sunu diggante." 
Ephesians2:15 Yoonu Musaa ak santaane yaak ndigal ya, moom la xewil, ngir yeesal ñaar ñi, Yawut beek jaambur bi, ci jenn jëmmu boppam, ñu doon kenn nit ku yees, ba jàmmoo." 
Ephesians2:16 Ñaar ñi la Almasi boole ci jenn jëmm, jubale leen ak Yàlla, ca bant ba ñu ko daajoon, te bant ba la dakkale sunub tongoo." 
Ephesians2:17 Moo dikke xibaaru jàmm buy yégle jàmm ju leen ñeel, yeen jaambur ñi ko sore woon, te ñeel nu, nun ñi ko jege," 
Ephesians2:18 ndax nun ñaari xeet yépp, ci moom Almasi lanu jote ci Baay bi, ci ndimbalal genn Noo gi." 
Ephesians2:19 Kon nag dootuleen ay gan mbaa ay doxandéem, waaye ay nawley ñu sell ñi ngeen, te waa kër Yàlla ngeen." 
Ephesians2:20 Yeena di tabax, bi ndawi Almasi ak yonent yi di kenu gi, te Almasi Yeesu ci boppam di doju coll wi." 
Ephesians2:21 Ci moom la tabax bi bépp di temboo, ba jóg, doon jaamookaay bu sell ngir Boroom bi." 
Ephesians2:22 Ci Almasi ngeen bokke ci tabax bi, yeen jaambur ñi itam, ba mana doon dëkkuwaayu Yàlla, ci ndimbalal Noo gu Sell gi." 
Ephesians3:1 Moo ma tax di ñaan, man Póol mi ñu tëj ngir Almasi, ndax ñi dul Yawut, yeen jaambur ñi," 
Ephesians3:2 ndegam yég ngeen sas wi ma Yàlla sas ciw yiwam, ñeel leen." 
Ephesians3:3 Ci am peeñu lañu ma xamale mbóot mi, noonu ma leen ko tënkale woon ci bataaxal." 
Ephesians3:4 Bu ngeen jàngee loolu, dingeen ràññee bu baax, ni ma dégge mbóot mi ci mbirum Almasi." 
Ephesians3:5 Moomu mbóot, xamaleesu ko woon doom aadama yi, ca janti maas ya woon, ni ñu ko feeñalale tey, ñu sell ñi diy ndawam ak yonent yi, ci ndimbalal Noo gu Sell gi," 
Ephesians3:6 ba mu leer ne jaambur ñi dul Yawut ñooy bokk ak Yawut yi benn cér bi, ñooy doon wenn yaram, te ñooy bokk benn dige bi ci Almasi Yeesu, ni ko xibaaru jàmm bi xamlee." 
Ephesians3:7 Xibaaru jàmm boobu lañu ma def ab jawriñam, te Yàlla, ciw yiwam, moo jëfe manooreem, ba jagleel ma boobu cér." 
Ephesians3:8 Man mi yées ci ñu sell ñépp lañu may woowu yiw, ba may xibaar jaambur ñi dul Yawut, xéewal yu amul kem yi ci Almasi." 
Ephesians3:9 May niital ñépp, ni Yàlla nara sottale mébétam, miy mbóot mu làqu woon naka jekk fa moom Yàlla mi sos lépp." 
Ephesians3:10 Su ko defee boroom nguur yeek boroom sañ-sañ ya fa déndi asamaan, mana xame ci mbooloom gëmkati Almasi, ni xelum Yàlla rafete ci wet gu nekk." 
Ephesians3:11 Loolu moo doon naka jekk nammeelam gi mu sottale ci Almasi Yeesu sunub Sang. 
Ephesians3:12 Ci Yeesu, ci kaw ngëm gu nu ko gëm lanu ñemee àgge fit wu mat sëkk, fa kanam Yàlla." 
Ephesians3:13 Kon nag dama leen di ñaan, ngeen baña yoqi ngir coono, yi may sonn ndax yeen; lépp seen teraanga la." 
Ephesians3:14 Looloo ma taxa sukk sama bëti óom, janook Baay bi," 
Ephesians3:15 ki gépp njabootug asamaan ak suuf, jële aw tur." 
Ephesians3:16 May ñaan nag, mu may leen, ci koomu teraangaam, seen jëmmu biir feddlikoo kàttanu Noowam gu Sell." 
Ephesians3:17 Su ko defee seen ngëm tax Almasi dëkke seen xol, ngeen sax ay reen yu sampe ci biir cofeel," 
Ephesians3:18 ngir yeen ak mboolem ñu sell ñi, seenum xel mana jàpp, ni mu leen ware, luy yaatuwaayub cofeelu Almasi, ak guddaay ba, ak kawewaay ba, ak xóotaay ba." 
Ephesians3:19 Ngeen boole ci daj cofeelu Almasi, gi wees xam-xam, ngir ngeen fees, ba fees dell ak koomu Yàlla." 
Ephesians3:20 Moom mi mana jëfoo kàttan giy liggéey ci nun, ba sottal mboolem lu nu ñaan ak lu nu xalaat, ba wees loola fuuf sax," 
Ephesians3:21 moo yelloo daraja ci biir mbooloom gëmkat ñi, ak ci Almasi Yeesu, tey ak ëllëg, ba fàww. Amiin." 
Ephesians4:1 Dama leen di dénku nag, man mi ñu tëj ndax Sang bi, ngir ngeen dund dundin wu yellook wooteb Yàlla, bi mu leen woo." 
Ephesians4:2 Saxooleen woyof, lewet, te deeleen muñ, di muñalante ngir cofeel." 
Ephesians4:3 Defleen seen kem kàttan, ngir di jàmmoo, ba mana sàmm seenug bennoo ci biir Noo gi ngeen bokk." 
Ephesians4:4 Wenn yaram a fi nekk, ak genn Noo, ak jenn yaakaar ju leen wooteb Yàlla jëme." 
Ephesians4:5 Benn Sang bi la it, ak genn ngëm, ak genn sóobu cim ndox." 
Ephesians4:6 Te it jenn Yàllaa am; mooy Baayu ñépp, moo tiim ñépp, di jëf ci ñépp te nekk ci ñépp." 
Ephesians4:7 Waaye ku nekk ci nun ak mayam, ci yiwu Yàlla, ni ko nattub Almasi séddalee." 
Ephesians4:8 Moo tax ñu ne: «Moo yéeg fa kawa kaw, yóbbaale gàngoor gu mu jàppe xare, te moo séddale nit ñi ay may.»" 
Ephesians4:9 Li ñu ne «moo yéeg,» ana lu mu tekki lu moy wàccoon na it ba fu gëna suufe?" 
Ephesians4:10 Kooku wàccoon mooy kenn ki yéegaat ba tiim asamaan yépp, ngir def lépp feese jëmmam." 
Ephesians4:11 Moo may ñii di ay ndawam, ñee di ay yonent, ñee di ay xamlekati xibaaru jàmm bi, ñale di ay sàmmi mbooloom gëmkat ñi, mbaa ay jànglekat." 
Ephesians4:12 Almasi moo waajale noonu ñu sell ñi, ba ñu mana bey seen sas ci liggéeyam, ngir tabax mbooloom gëmkat, mi taxawe yaramu Almasi." 
Ephesians4:13 Su ko defee nu mana màgg nun ñépp ba doon benn ci ngëm, ak ci xam-xam bu mat ci Doomu Yàlla ji, ba kera nuy doon magum jëmm, bay tollook taxawaayu Almasi bi mat sëkk." 
Ephesians4:14 Su boobaa nu noppee doon ay tuut-tànk yu nit ñiy muusaatoo kàddu yu mel ni gannax yu nuy baaje, ak ngelawal mboolem àlluwa ju bees ju nuy pamti-pamtee ci seen biir pexey naxe ak njublaŋ, ngir fàbbi nu." 
Ephesians4:15 Su boobaa kay, dëgg gu nu wodde cofeel lanuy wéye, tey màgg ci bépp fànn, ci moom Almasi miy bopp bi." 
Ephesians4:16 Ci moom miy bopp bi la yaram wépp di déggoo, témboo ndax ndimbalal mboolem tenqo yi koy saytu, na mu dëppook wàllu cér bu ci nekk. Su ko defee yaram wiy yokku, di màgg ci biir cofeel." 
Ephesians4:17 Lii nag maa leen ko wax, te di ko biral ci turu Boroom bi: Ni xeeti yéefar yiy jëfe, topp seen xalaat yu tekkiwul dara, buleen jëfeeti noonu." 
Ephesians4:18 Seenum xel a tàbbi ag lëndëm, ñu tumurànke dundin wi Yàlla di maye, te umple gi ci ñoom moo tax, ndax seenug dëgër bopp." 
Ephesians4:19 Dañoo mujj dërkiis, yebu ci topp seen bakkan, ba xaabaabal ci jépp jëfi sobe." 
Ephesians4:20 Yeen nag du loolu ngeen jànge ci Almasi," 
Ephesians4:21 ndegam kay Yeesu ci boppam ngeen dégg mbiram, ba jànge ci moom, dëgg gi bawoo ci moom," 
Ephesians4:22 te mooy ngeen ba seen jikko ju jëkk ja, ngeen teqlikoo ak seen jëmmu démb ja masa topp bànneexi bakkan yuy naxe, ba sóobu ci yàqute." 
Ephesians4:23 Su ko defee ngeen mana yeeslu ci seenum xel, ci ndimbalal Noo gi," 
Ephesians4:24 te ngeen soloo jëmm ju yees ji Yàlla sàkke ci takkndeeram, di jëfe njub, ak sellnga ji dëgg di jur." 
Ephesians4:25 Kon nag bàyyileen fen, te ku nekk di wax sa moroom, dëgg, ndax ku nekk ci yeen sab céru moroom nga." 
Ephesians4:26 Buleen mer ba bàkkaar, te bu jant bi sowe seen mer;" 
Ephesians4:27 buleen xajal Seytaane. 
Ephesians4:28 Sàcc bi, na ba sàcc te nangoo sonn, di liggéeye loxoom liggéey bu rafet, ba man cee dimbali néew-ji-doole ji." 
Ephesians4:29 Bu genn kàddu gu bon génne seen gémmiñ, xanaa su ko jaree ngeen wax lu baax, luy jariñe, te diw yiw ci ñi koy dégg." 
Ephesians4:30 Te it buleen tiisal Noowug Yàlla gu Sell, gi leen màndargaale xàmmikaayam ngir bésub njot ba." 
Ephesians4:31 Lépp luy wextan, ak naqari deret, ak mer mu ëpp, ak coow, ak wax ju ñaaw, na lépp buube, ba génne ci seen biir, mook mboolem jëfi coxor." 
Ephesians4:32 Baaxleen ci seen diggante, di ñeewantante, tey balante, ni leen Yàlla baale ci Almasi." 
Ephesians5:1 Kon nag doonleen ay roykati Yàlla, gannaaw yeenay doomam yi mu sopp," 
Ephesians5:2 te ngeen di doxale cofeel, ni Almasi mi nu sopp, ba jooxeel nu bakkanam, def ko saraxu sawara, ngir xetug jàmm, ñeel Yàlla." 
Ephesians5:3 Lu jëm nag ci powum séy, ak jépp jëfi sobe, mbaa ag bëgge, li jekk ci ay nit ñu sell, moo di ñu bañ koo tudd sax ci seen biir," 
Ephesians5:4 te ag ñàkk kersa, ak waxi caaxaan, ak kaf yu bon, dara jekku ci, waaye saxooleen kàdduy cant." 
Ephesians5:5 Ndax lii kat na leen wóor: képp ku nekke powum séy, mbaa jëfi sobe, mbaa ag bëgge, kooku amul cér ci nguurug Almasi ak Yàlla, ndax ku bëgge ab bokkaalekat la." 
Ephesians5:6 Bu leen kenn naxe waxi ngelawal neen, ndax yooyu ma lim mooy wàcce sànjum Yàlla ci kaw aji déggadi ñi." 
Ephesians5:7 Kon nag buleen séq ak ñooñu dara. 
Ephesians5:8 Ag lëndëm ngeen woon démb, waaye tey ag leer ngeen ci Boroom bi ngeen bokk. Jëfeleen nag ni niti leer." 
Ephesians5:9 Li leer gi ci yeen di meññ moo di mboolem luy mbaax ak njub ak dëgg. 
Ephesians5:10 Ràññeeleen li neex Boroom bi; 
Ephesians5:11 jëfi lëndëm amul njariñ, buleen ci bokk, xanaa ngeen feeñal ñaawtéefu jëf ja." 
Ephesians5:12 Ndax kat li nit ñooñu di làquy def, waxtaane ko sax, lu ruslu la." 
Ephesians5:13 Waaye mboolem lu ñu feeñal, leer ga ñu ko leerale moo ko wone," 
Ephesians5:14 te lépp lu ñu wone ci ag leer, di ag leer. Moo tax ñu ne: «Yaw miy nelaw, yewwul, dekkil, Almasi leeral la.»" 
Ephesians5:15 Kon nag xool-leen bu baax seen jëfin, defleen jëfinu nit ñu am xel, te baña mel ni ñu ñàkk xel," 
Ephesians5:16 Jariñooleen lu ngeen man, jot gi ngeen amagum, ndax jant yu bona ngii tey." 
Ephesians5:17 Moo tax buleen def jëfi ñàkk bopp, waaye jéemleena xam coobarey Boroom bi." 
Ephesians5:18 Buleen naan biiñ ba màndi, màndite ci afal seen bakkan la leen jëme, waaye na leen Noo gi fees," 
Ephesians5:19 ngeen di jàngalante jàngi Sabóor, ak jàngi cant, ak jàng yu bawoo ci Noo gi leen fees, te ngeen di woy aka kañ Boroom bi, ci seen xol." 
Ephesians5:20 Fu ngeen tollu, ak ci mbir mu mu mana doon, santleen Yàlla Baay bi ci sunu turu Sang Yeesu Almasi," 
Ephesians5:21 te ngeen rus Almasi, ba tax ngeen di nangulante." 
Ephesians5:22 Na jabar nangul jëkkëram ni mu nangule Sang bi. 
Ephesians5:23 Almasi moo di musalkatu mbooloom gëmkat ñi, mbooloo mi di aw yaramam. Te itam ni Almasi dee boppu mbooloom gëmkat ñi, ni la jëkkër ji dee boppu jabaram." 
Ephesians5:24 Kon nag ni mbooloo mi nangule Almasi, ni la jabar ji wara nangule jëkkëram ci lépp." 
Ephesians5:25 Jëkkër nag, na sopp jabaram ni Almasi soppe mbooloom gëmkat ñi, ba jooxeel leen bakkanam." 
Ephesians5:26 Moo defal loolu mbooloo mi ba man koo setale cangaayal ndox mu ànd ak kàddoom, ngir sellal ko." 
Ephesians5:27 Li mu ci namm moo di teewal mbooloo mi fi kanamam, mu mel ni ab séetam bu ne ràññ, gàkkul, rasul, taqul lenn, xanaa sell, mucc sikk." 
Ephesians5:28 Noonu la jëkkër ji wara soppe jabaram, ni mu soppe yaramu boppam rekk. Sopp sa jabar sopp sa bopp la," 
Ephesians5:29 ndax kenn masula bañ suuxu boppam, xanaa mu di ko dundal, di ko topptoo, ni Almasi ak mbooloom gëmkat ñi," 
Ephesians5:30 nde noo di céri yaramam. 
Ephesians5:31 Ni ko Mbind mi indee: «Looloo tax góor di bàyyikoo ci ndeyam ak baayam, daldi taqoo ak jabaram, ba ñoom ñaar di wenn suux.»" 
Ephesians5:32 Mbóot mu xóota ngi ci dog boobu, waaye man, li may wax moo di dog bi moo misaal diggante, bi Almasi séq ak mbooloo mi." 
Ephesians5:33 Teewuleen koo moom yeen itam; kon na ku nekk sopp jabaram ni mu soppe boppam, te ku nekk weg jëkkëram." 
Ephesians6:1 Naka yeen xale yi, déggal-leen seeni waajur, ngir Boroom bi, ndax moo war." 
Ephesians6:2 «Teral-leen seen ndey ak seen baay,» mooy ndigal li jëkka ànd akub dige," 
Ephesians6:3 ndax da ne: «ngir ngeen baaxle te gudd fan ci kaw suuf.» 
Ephesians6:4 Yeen ñiy baay it, buleen xoñoñal xale yi, waaye yarleen leen, di leen jubanti, di leen xamal coobarey Boroom bi." 
Ephesians6:5 Yeen jaam yi, déggal-leen seen sangi àddina, ànd ceek ragal Yàlla bay kat-kati, ak xol bu dëggu. Ni ngeen déggale Almasi, nangeen leen ni déggale." 
Ephesians6:6 Buleen ko defe ngistal, mbaa ngeen di ko sàkkoo lu leen neex, na di yéene ju ngeen tibbe ci seen xol, ngir jëfe liy coobarey Yàlla, ni mu ware ay jaami Almasi." 
Ephesians6:7 Liggéeyal-leen leen ci xol bu tàlli, ba mu mel ni Boroom bi ngeen ko defal, waaye du nit doŋŋ," 
Ephesians6:8 te ngeen xam ne nit ki, mu dis gor mbaa ab jaam, mboolem lu mu def ci lu baax, loola la ko Boroom biy delloo." 
Ephesians6:9 Yeen it sang yi, jëfeleen noonu seen diggante ak seeni jaam, bàyyileen di tëkkoo, te ngeen xam ne yeen ak ñoom a bokk benn Boroom fa asamaan, te xejj ak seen amul fa moom." 
Ephesians6:10 Li ci des nag moo di ngeen manoorewoo Boroom bi, te ngeen sàkkoo ndimbal ci dooleem ak kàttanam gi amul kem." 
Ephesians6:11 Ràngooleen mboolem gànnaayi Yàlla, ngir ngeen mana jànkoonte ak pexey Seytaane." 
Ephesians6:12 Ndax kat sunub xare du nook boroomi deret ak suux, waaye ñi ñu ko séqal ay boroom nguur lañu, ak ay boroom sañ-sañ, ak ay boroom doole yu nekk ci àddina ju lëndëm jii, di ay dagi Seytaane yu fare déndi asamaan." 
Ephesians6:13 Kon nag jël-leen gànnaayi Yàlla yépp, ba bu bésub safaan taxawee, ngeen mana jëflante, ba sottal, tey wéye taxaw temm." 
Ephesians6:14 Taxawleen kon temm. Defleen dëgg di ngañaay li ci seen ndigg, njub di seen kiiraayal dënn." 
Ephesians6:15 Xibaaru jàmm bi indi jàmm nag, defleen ko muy dàll yu dëgëral seen taxawaay." 
Ephesians6:16 Te fu ngeen tollu ŋàbbleen pakk biy seen ngëm, ci ngeen mana fanqe mboolem jumi sawaray ku Bon ki." 
Ephesians6:17 Mbaxanam xare miy seen kaaraange, jël-leen ko, sol, jël-leen itam saamar bi Noo giy joxe, te muy kàddug Yàlla." 
Ephesians6:18 Deeleen ñaan fu ngeen tollu, gépp xeetu ñaan aki dagaan ci ndimbalal Noo gi, ànd ci ak teewlu fu ngeen tollu, ak gépp farlute, te ngeen di ñaanal mboolem gëmkat ñu sell ñi." 
Ephesians6:19 Man itam, booleleen ma ci, ngir saa yu ma ubbee sama gémmiñ, mana xéewloo ndéey lu ma xamlee fit wu dëgër, mbóoti xibaaru jàmm bi," 
Ephesians6:20 xibaar bi ma di ndawam lu ñu tënke ay jéng. Waaye ñaanal-leen ma ma di ko waxee fit, ni mu ma ware." 
Ephesians6:21 Dingeen mana xam nag lu jëm ci man, ak li may def, ndax Tisig, mbokk mu ñu sopp, jawriñ ju wóor ci liggéeyu Boroom bi, moo leen di xamal lépp." 
Ephesians6:22 Loolu ci boppam sax moo waral ma yónni ko ci yeen, ngir mu xamal leen ni nu nekke, ba seral seen xol." 
Ephesians6:23 Yal na jàmm ñeel bokki gëmkat ñi, ak cofeel gu ànd ak ngëm, bawoo fa Yàlla Baay bi, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
Ephesians6:24 Na aw yiw ñeel mboolem ñi sopp sunu Sàng Yeesu Almasi, cofeel gu dul fey." 
Philippians1:1 Man la Póol, Timote miy jaamub Almasi Yeesu ni man ànd ak man ci lii, ñeel mboolem ñu sell ñi gëm Almasi Yeesu, te dëkke Filib, yeen ak seeni njiit ak taxawukati mbooloo mi." 
Philippians1:2 Aw yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen, bawoo fa sunu Baay, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
Philippians1:3 Damay sant Yàlla saa Boroom saa yu ma leen fàttlikoo," 
Philippians1:4 te saa su ma leen di ñaanal, mbég laa leen di ñaanale yeen ñépp," 
Philippians1:5 ndax seen loxo bi ngeen jo ci xamle xibaaru jàmm bi, te dale ko ca bés bu jëkk ba ba tey." 
Philippians1:6 Te lii kat, bir na ma; ki tàmbali jii jëf ju baax ci yeen, dina ko àggale ba keroog bésub Almasi Yeesu." 
Philippians1:7 Maa yey nag njortal leen loolu yeen ñépp, ndax ci sama xol laa leen def, te it muy ci wàllu jéng yi ñu ma jénge, di ci wàllu kàddu guy waxal xibaaru jàmm bi, ak di ko feddli, yeen ñépp am ngeen wàll ci sama añub yiw." 
Philippians1:8 Yàlla seede na ne sopp naa leen yeen ñépp, cofeel gu Almasi Yeesu ci boppam àttana tibbe ci biir xolam." 
Philippians1:9 Li may ñaan nag moo di seen cofeel yokku tey gën di yokku, te ngeen ànd ceek xam-xam bu matale ak gépp ràññee," 
Philippians1:10 ba mana xàmmi li gën. Su ko defee ngeen set wecc te mucc sikk, ngir keroog bésub Almasi." 
Philippians1:11 Su boobaa ngeen meññal ba woomle ci njub, gi Yeesu Almasi di maye, ngir fésal màggug Yàlla, jollil ag cantam." 
Philippians1:12 Damaa bëgg, bokk yi, ngeen xam ne lii ma dal, xibaaru jàmm bi la far jëmale kanam." 
Philippians1:13 Ndax kat, bir na mboolem dagi boroom dëkk bi te bir na ñeneen ñépp ne Almasee tax ñu jéng ma." 
Philippians1:14 Te it li gëna bare ci bokki gëmkat ñi, sama jéng yi ma nekke nii moo leen yokk aw fit, ba tax ñu gëna ñemee waxe kàddu gi te ragaluñu ci dara." 
Philippians1:15 Dëgg la am na ñuy waare turu Almasi ci kaw kiñaan ak diiroo mbagg, waaye am na itam ñu koy defe yéene ju rafet." 
Philippians1:16 Ñooñu cofeel a leen tax di waare, ndax xam nañu ne waxal xibaaru jàmm bi laa sasoo." 
Philippians1:17 Waaye ñale, xelum wujje lañuy siiwtaanee Almasi, du yéene ju rafet ju ñu ci am, xanaa defe ne seeni pexe man na maa yokk coono ci diggante bii ñu ma jénge." 
Philippians1:18 Ana lu ci topp nag? Ba tey rekk, ak nu mu mana deme, muy waareb jinigal, mbaa waare bu dëggu, turu Almasi moo ci jollee, muy sama mbégtem tey, dellu di sama mbégtem ëllëg," 
Philippians1:19 ndax xam naa ne loolu lépp ay walbatiku di samag mucc, ndax seeni ñaan, ak ndimbalal Noowug Yeesu Almasi." 
Philippians1:20 Loolu laa ne siiw, yaakaar ko, te duma rus mukk, xanaa di saxoo aw fit, démb niki tey, ngir ma mana fésale sama jëmm jépp, teddngay Almasi, su may dund ak su may dee." 
Philippians1:21 Ndax samag dund, Almasi la ñeel, samag dee dàqati." 
Philippians1:22 Su dee nag damaa wara wéye sama bakkan bii, ngir mana sottal ab liggéey bu am njariñ, ana lu ma gënal ci diggante dund ak dee? Xawma ko." 
Philippians1:23 Ci diggante yaar yooyii laa tance: yàkkamti na maa yiwiku ba fekki Almasi, te loolu moo dàqati fuuf." 
Philippians1:24 Waaye ma deseegum bakkan moo gëna jamp ci yeen. 
Philippians1:25 Gannaaw loolu bir na ma nag, xam naa ne dinaa desagum, desandoo feek yeen ñépp, ngir ngeen jëm kanam, tey bége seen ngëm," 
Philippians1:26 ba bu ma délsee fi yeen, ngeen gëna mana puukarewoo Almasi Yeesu ndax man." 
Philippians1:27 Fexeleen rekk ba di jëfe ni mu yelloo ak xibaaru jàmm bu Almasi, ngir bu ma leen seetsee, mana seede, mbaa su ma wuutee it, di dégg ni ngeen saxoo di mànkoo, bokk jenn yéene, di xeex ngir saxal ngëm gi sukkandiku ci xibaaru jàmm bi." 
Philippians1:28 Buleen ragal seeni noon ci lenn. Seen fit mooy màndargaal sànkutey noon yi, te yeen it, mooy màndargaal seenug mucc gu bawoo fa Yàlla." 
Philippians1:29 Ndax kat yeen la may ci jëmmu Almasi, yiwu gëm Almasi, rax ci dolli, ngeen sonn ndax moom," 
Philippians1:30 coonoy benn xare bi ngeen bokk ak man, te gise woon ma ko démb, ba tey, ngeen di ma ko dégge." 
Philippians2:1 Ndegam amees na lenn lu yokk aw fit ci Almasi mi nu gëm, ndegam lenni cofeelam lu mana dëfal am na, ndegam amees na benn cér ci Noo gu Sell gi, ndegam it, amees na lenn lu bawoo fi moom, ci wàllu xol bu rafet, ak yërmande," 
Philippians2:2 kon dëgg waay, mottlileen sama mbég, ba mànkoo, te ngeen soppantee genn cofeel, jubale seeni xol, te bokk benn jëmu." 
Philippians2:3 Buleen def dara ci kaw wujje, mbaa réy-réylu, waaye doyadiluleen, ba jàpp ne seen moroomi gëmkat a leen gën." 
Philippians2:4 Bu kenn ci yeen xintewoo njariñal boppam, waaye na ku nekk bàyyi xel moroomam." 
Philippians2:5 Noonu Almasi Yeesu doon doxale, deeleen ko doxale ci seen biir:" 
Philippians2:6 Moom mi nekke nekkinu Yàlla te ŋoyaaloowul dayob boppam, bi ko def nawleb Yàlla." 
Philippians2:7 Xanaa mu ŋacc boppam, nangoo jagoo nekkinu surga. Mu mujj mel ni nit doŋŋ, di ku ñu xàmmee jëmmu nitam." 
Philippians2:8 Moo toroxlu, moo nangu, ba dee fekk ko ci, ak mbugalu bant ba ñu ko daaj." 
Philippians2:9 Moo tax Yàlla kaweel koo kaweel, baaxe ko tur wi tiim wépp tur," 
Philippians2:10 ba turu Yeesu tax ñépp sukk seen bëti óom, muy kaw asamaan, di kaw suuf, di biir suuf," 
Philippians2:11 làmmiñu ñépp it biral ne Yeesu Almasi mooy Sang bi, te muy ndamu Yàlla Baay bi." 
Philippians2:12 Kon nag soppe yi, noonu ngeen masa dégge ndigal, démb ba may teew, rawatina tey bi ma wuutee, nangeen ko wéye, di jëfe seenug mucc, te ànd ceek ragal Yàlla bay lox," 
Philippians2:13 ndax Yàlla mooy liggéey ci yeen lu tax ngeen mana namma jëfe coobareem, ba man koo jëfe." 
Philippians2:14 Mboolem lu ngeen di def nag, buleen ci boole xultu mbaa xuloo," 
Philippians2:15 ngir seen der set wecc, te kon deesuleen mana gàkkal ci lenn. Ay goney Yàlla yu amul sikk ngeen di doon, ci biir maas gu dëng te yàqu, ngeen di lerxat ci seen biir, ni ay leer ci àddina si," 
Philippians2:16 ànd ak kàddug dund gi ngeen di xamle. Su ko defee keroog bésub Almasi, ma mana damoo ne dawuma cig neen, te sonnuma cig neen." 
Philippians2:17 Su ma ci deeyee sax, ba sama dund mel ni sarax su ñu tuur, tofal ko ci sarax, bi seen ngëm taxawe, su boobaa it maa ciy bég, te di leen woo, ngir bokk ak yeen ñépp bànneexu." 
Philippians2:18 Yeen itam nangeen ci bég te bokk ak man bànneexu. 
Philippians2:19 Yaakaar naa nag, ne bu soobee Sang Yeesu, dinaa leen yónnee Timote balaa yàgg, ngir xam nu ngeen def, ba man ci sama bopp, sama xel dal." 
Philippians2:20 Ndaxte awma fi kenn ku ko moy, ku bokk ak man xinte, ba seeni mbir yitteel ko dëgg." 
Philippians2:21 Ñi ci des ñépp, seen njariñal bopp lañuy sàkku, waaye du li soxal Yeesu Almasi." 
Philippians2:22 Timote nag xam ngeen ne ku rafet ab jëw la. Ni doom di taxawoo baayam, ni la bokke ak man liggéey, bi ci xamle xibaaru jàmm bi." 
Philippians2:23 Sama yaakaar nag moo di, bu may am lu leer ci sama mbir rekk, moom laay daldi yebal ci yeen." 
Philippians2:24 Teewul mu bir ma ne, bu soobee Boroom bi, man ci sama bopp, balaa yàgg, dinaa leen seetsi." 
Philippians2:25 Ci wàllu Epafrodit, sama mbokkum gëmkat la, di sama naataango, di sama mbokkum xarekat, te di seen ndaw li ngeen ma yóbbante ndimbal lu faj samay soxla. Waaye jàpp naa ne fàww ma delloo leen ko," 
Philippians2:26 ndax namm na leen lool, boole ci tiisoo li ngeen dégg ag jagadeem." 
Philippians2:27 Woppoon na it ba xawa dee, waaye Yàllaa ko yërëm, te du moom rekk la yërëm, waaye man itam, ngir ma baña am tiis ci kaw tiis." 
Philippians2:28 Moo tax ma yàkkamtileen koo delloo, ngir bu dikkee, ngeen man koo bégewaat, te man itam, samaw tiis wàññiku." 
Philippians2:29 Teertooleen ko mbégte mu mat sëkk ngir Sang bi, te it nawleen ñu mel ni moom," 
Philippians2:30 ndax liggéeyal Almasi tax na koo riisu ndee; ba ngeen amee ngànt lu leen teree mottlil seen bopp, seen yéene, moo jaay bakkanam ngir wuutu leen, ba yótsi ma seen ndimbal." 
Philippians3:1 Li ci des bokk yi, ma waxati, bégleen ci Boroom bi. Di leen bind genn kàddu googu rekk, diisu ma, te di leen ko baamtu moo gëna wóor ci yeen." 
Philippians3:2 Moytuleen xaj yi, defkati mbon yooyu laa ne, moytuleen leen, moytuleen njoofkat yooyu jiital aaday xaraf." 
Philippians3:3 Ndaxte nun noo xaraf tigi, nun ñiy jaamoo Yàlla Noowam gu Sell, di damoo Almasi Yeesu, te yaakaarunu aaday nitu suuxu neen." 
Philippians3:4 Moona man de, waroon naa mana yaakaar aaday suuxu neen. Ak keneen ku mana xalaat ne sañ naa yaakaar aaday nitu suuxu neen, maa ci raw." 
Philippians3:5 Man mi xaraf ba ma amee juróom ñetti fan, askanoo ci bànni Israyil, giiroo ci Beñamin, di ab Ebrë bu ñaari Ebrë jur, te bokk ci ngérum Farisen, ci wàllu yoonu Musaa." 
Philippians3:6 Su dee ci mbirum xéraangey diine, maa daan bundxatal mbooloom gëmkati Almasi, te su dee ci wàllu njubtey sàmm yoon wi, maa mucc sikk." 
Philippians3:7 Waaye la ma jàppe woon ag ndollant, moom laa def tey ag wàññeent ndax Almasi." 
Philippians3:8 Rax ci dolli, lépp sax laa far jàppe ag wàññeent, ndax ngëneel li sut lépp, te mooy xam kuy sama Sang Almasi Yeesu. Moom moo ma taxa nangoo ñàkk lépp, def lépp ni mbuubit, ngir tonoo Almasi," 
Philippians3:9 ngir ma mana feeñe ci biir Almasi, fu ma yaakaarul sama njekku bopp gu ma feyoo sàmm yoonu Musaa, xanaa di yaakaar njekk gu laloo ngëm gi ma gëm Almasi. Njekk googu fa Yàlla la bawoo te gëm Almasi moo koy maye." 
Philippians3:10 Sàkkuwuma lu moy xam ko, xam manoore ji ko dekkal, ak itam séddu ci ay coonoom, ba bokk ak moom deeyam," 
Philippians3:11 tey yaakaara dekki, ak nu mu mana deme." 
Philippians3:12 Du caageenu damaa àgg ci loolu lépp ba noppi, mbaa damaa mat sëkk xaat, waaye maa ngi wéye samaw xél, di jéema jot ci neexalu rawante bi, gannaaw ba ma Almasi Yeesu jotee ci man itam." 
Philippians3:13 Bokk yi, fooguma ne jot naa ci, xanaa kay lenn: damay fàtte li ci gannaaw, te def lu ma man, ngir fexee yóotuji li ci kanam," 
Philippians3:14 daldi xélu dëgmal naanukaay ba, ngir jot ca neexal ba nu Yàlla di wooye fa kaw, ci Almasi Yeesu." 
Philippians3:15 Kon nag, nun ñi jota màgg ba di magi jëmm ci wàllu ngëm, nanu ko bokk gise noonu. Su ci amee lenn lu ngeen gise neneen nag, loola, Yàlla moo leen koy leeralal." 
Philippians3:16 Ak lu ci mana am, yoon wii nu doxe ba fii nu tollu, nanu ko bokk topp." 
Philippians3:17 Bokk yi, royleen ma; jox nanu leen ab royukaay, xool-leen ci ñi koy jëfe, te ngeen topp ci seeni tànk." 
Philippians3:18 Ndaxte ñu baree ngii ñu seeni jëf tax ñu di nooni bantub Almasi. Loolu wax naa leen ko ay yoon, ma waxati leen ko tey aki jooy." 
Philippians3:19 Ñooñu sànkute lañuy mujje; seen koll lañu def seen yàlla, seen gàcce lañuy damoo, te yëfi àddina doŋŋ a leen soxal." 
Philippians3:20 Nun nag sunum réew a nga fa asamaan, fa nuy séentoo sunu Musalkat, Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
Philippians3:21 Mooy kiy liggéeye manooreem ji mu tënke lépp cig curgaam, ba sopparñi sunu yaram wu doyadi wii, nirule kook yaramam wi ànd ak teddnga." 
Philippians4:1 Kon nag yeen samay bokk, soppe yi ma namm, di leen bége, te ngeen di sama kaalag ndam, gi ma yooloo ci sama liggéey, ngalla soppe yi, nangeen saxe noonu ci Boroom bi!" 
Philippians4:2 Bu loolu weesee, Ewodi laay tinu, di tinu Santis, ñaari jigéen ñooñu, ngir ñu fexe ba juboo, ngir Boroom bi ñu bokk." 
Philippians4:3 Yaw itam sama mbokkum surga bu dëggu bi, dama lay ñaan nga jàpple leen ci, ñoom ñaar ñooñoo bokkoon ak man coonob xamle xibaaru jàmm bi, ñoom ak ñoom Kelemaŋ, mboolem sama bokki liggéeykat yi seeni tur binde ca téereb dund ba." 
Philippians4:4 Bégleen ci Boroom bi fu ngeen tollu, ma waxati ko, bégleen!" 
Philippians4:5 Na seen lewetaay wóor ñépp, Sang bi jegesi na." 
Philippians4:6 Buleen jaaxle ci dara, waaye ci mbir mu mu mana doon, deeleen dikke Yàlla seeni soxla, di ko ñaan ak a dagaan te boole ci di ko sant." 
Philippians4:7 Su boobaa jàmmu Yàlla, ji wees ab takk, mooy sàmm seen xol, ak seenum xel ndax Almasi Yeesu." 
Philippians4:8 Li ci des nag bokk yi, moo di lii: mboolem lu dëggu, ak mboolem lu tedd, ak mboolem luy njub, ak mboolem lu set, ak mboolem lu jekk, ak mboolem lees di rafetlu, ndegam lu nawlu la te yelloo ngërëm, na leen loola soxal." 
Philippians4:9 Li ngeen jànge ci man te jële ko ci man, ak li ngeen dégge ci man, gise ko ci man, jëfeleen ko. Su boobaa Yàlla miy boroom jàmm mooy ànd ak yeen." 
Philippians4:10 Maa ngi bége Boroom bi lool ci nii ngeen mujj yeesale tey, seen yitte ci man, yitte ju ngeen amoon moos naka jekk, xanaa dangeena ñàkkoona jekku seen ndimbal." 
Philippians4:11 Ag ñàkk nag taxul may waxe nii, nde tàmm naa di doylu ci diggante bu ma mana tollu." 
Philippians4:12 Miin naa néewle, man naa naataange. Fépp fu ma tollu, ak ci lépp, làqoo naa pexe mu ma manee jant yu ma regge, ak yu ma xiife, ci biir naataange akug ñàkk." 
Philippians4:13 Lépp laa mane ci ndimbalal Ki may manal. 
Philippians4:14 Teewul seen ndimbal lii di jëf ju rafet ju ngeen bokke ak man, sama njàqare." 
Philippians4:15 Yeen waa Filib, xam ngeen xéll ne ba waareb xibaaru jàmm bay door, te ma bàyyikoo diiwaanu Masedwan, amul woon menn mbooloom gëmkat mu ma séqaloon ab joqlanteb ndimbal, xanaa seen mennum mbooloo." 
Philippians4:16 Ba ma nekkee Tesalonig sax, yónnee ngeen ma ay yoon, lu ma faje samay soxla." 
Philippians4:17 Du caageenu ndimbal lu ma leen di sàkku, li may sàkku kay moo di yokkuteb yool bu leen ñeel." 
Philippians4:18 Fii ma tollu jot naa li ma aajowoo lépp, maa ngi ci naataange; doyle naa sëkk, gannaaw ba ma nangoo ci loxol Epafrodit, seenub yóbbante, te sarax su ñu nangu la, di xeeñ xetug jàmm, te neex Yàlla mi mu ñeel." 
Philippians4:19 Te sama Yàlla itam mooy sàkke ci koomam gu yéeme gi ci Almasi Yeesu, ba fajal leen seen soxla yépp." 
Philippians4:20 Daraja ñeel na Yàlla sunu Baay, tey ak ëllëg ba fàww. Amiin." 
Philippians4:21 Nuyul-leen ma mboolem ñu sell ñi gëm Almasi Yeesu. Bokki gëmkat ñi ànd ak man, ñu ngi leen di nuyu." 
Philippians4:22 Te it gëmkat ñu sell ñépp a ngi leen di nuyu, rawatina waa kër Buur Sesaar." 
Philippians4:23 Yal na yiwu Sang Yeesu Almasi ànd ak seenum xel. 
Colossians1:1 Man Póol ndawal Almasi Yeesu ci coobarey Yàlla, maa bind lii, ànd ceek mbokk mi Timote," 
Colossians1:2 ñeel waa Kolos ñu sell te wóor te di bokki gëmkati Almasi. Aw yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen, bawoo fa Yàlla sunu Baay." 
Colossians1:3 Sant Yàlla sunu Baayu Sang Yeesu Almasi, lanu saxoo, saa su nu leen di ñaanal;" 
Colossians1:4 dégg nanu ngëm gi ngeen gëm Almasi Yeesu, ak cofeel gi ngeen sopp gëmkat ñu sell ñépp," 
Colossians1:5 te li waral ngëm googu ak cofeel googu, di seen yaakaara jot ca cér ba ñu leen dencal fa asamaan. Mooy yaakaar ja ngeen dale am ba ngeen jëkkee dégg kàddug dëgg gu xibaaru jàmm bi." 
Colossians1:6 Ni leen xibaaru jàmm bi dikkale nag, ni la dikkale àddina sépp, te mu ngi meññ, di law, na mu ko dale defe fi seen biir, ca bés ba ngeen déggee lu jëm ci yiwu Yàlla, ba ràññee ko dëgg." 
Colossians1:7 Noonu ngeen ko jànge ci Epafras, sunu mbokkum surga biy sunu soppe, te di jawriñu Almasi bu wóor bi nu jàpple," 
Colossians1:8 te moo nu xamal itam cofeel gi leen Noo gi may. 
Colossians1:9 Moo tax nun itam, ba nu déggee seen mbir ba tey, noppiwunu leena ñaanal, di sàkku ngeen feese xam-xam ci lépp luy coobarey Yàlla, te ngeen ànd ceek lu mat sëkk ci wàllu xel, ak gis-gis bu Noo gi maye." 
Colossians1:10 Su ko defee ngeen di dunde dundin wu yellook Boroom bi, ngir bànneexal ko ci wet gu nekk, seen meññeef it di jépp jëf ju baax, te ngeen gën di xam Yàlla." 
Colossians1:11 Ngir itam ngeen manoorewoo jépp manoore, na leen ko Yàlla manloo ci kàttanam gu màgg, ba ngeen mana dékkoo lépp, xolu muñ," 
Colossians1:12 te ngeen di sante Baay bi, mbég, moom mi leen yellale ab cér ca muuru ñu sell ña, ca réewum leer ga." 
Colossians1:13 Yàlla kat moo nu wallu ba génne nu ca kilifteefu réewum lëndëm ga, toxal nu ci biir nguurug Doomam ji mu sopp." 
Colossians1:14 Ci moom lanu ame ag njot, te moo nu jéggal sunuy bàkkaar." 
Colossians1:15 Doom jooju moo di niruwaale Yàlla, mi kenn manula gis, mooy taaw bi, ki jiitu mépp mbindeef." 
Colossians1:16 Ndax moo di ki Yàlla sàkke lépp lu nekk asamaan, ak lu nekk ci suuf, lu gisu, ak lu gisuwul, muy boroom gàngune yeek, boroom ndomboy tànk yeek, boroom nguur yeek, boroom sañ-sañ yi. Lépp ci moom lees ko sàkke, te mooy ki tax ñu sàkk lépp." 
Colossians1:17 Mooy ki nekkoon naka jekk balaa daraa nekk, te lépp ci moom la sottee ba temboo." 
Colossians1:18 Mooy boppu yaram, wiy mbooloom gëmkat ñi, mooy njàlbéen, mooy taaw bi jëkka dekki, ndekkite lu dee toppul, ba tax muy ki jiitu ci lépp," 
Colossians1:19 ndax Yàlla la soob mu dëël gépp matam ci moom. 
Colossians1:20 Deretam ja tuuru ca bant ba, ca la Yàlla defe jàmm, ba sottale ci moom, pexe mi mu jubalee boppam ak lépp, muy lu nekk ci kaw suuf, ak la fa asamaan." 
Colossians1:21 Te yeen ñi masoona sore lool Yàlla, doonoon ay noonam ci wàllu xalaat, ak jëf ju bon," 
Colossians1:22 tey, deewug yaram, deewug suux, gi Almasi dee, moom la leen Yàlla jubalee ak boppam, ba teewal leen fi kanamam, ngeen di ñu sell, mucc sikk, seen der set wecc." 
Colossians1:23 Noonu la deme, ndegam kay fekk na leen sësoo ngëm gu ngeen dëjoo ba dëgër, te baña nangu lenn di leen sorele ak yaakaar ji ci xibaaru jàmm, bi ngeen dégg, te ñu biral ko, ñeel mépp mbindeef. Man Póol nag, ci yégle xibaaru jàmm boobu laa di ab jawriñ." 
Colossians1:24 Léegi nag maa ngi bége coono yi ma jànkoonteel ngir seen njariñ; li des ci tiisi Almasi, moom laay mottalee coono yooyu ma daje sama yaramu suux wii, ngir njariñal mbooloom gëmkat, miy yaramu Almasi." 
Colossians1:25 Ci moomu mbooloo laa dib jawriñ, te Yàllaa ma sase noonu, ñeel leen, ngir ma xamle kàddug Yàlla ba mu mat sëkk." 
Colossians1:26 Kàddu googu moo di mbóot mi masoona làqu maasoo maas, waaye tey Yàllaa ko xamal ay nitam ñu sell." 
Colossians1:27 Ñoom la Yàlla nammoona xamal ni mbóot mi yaatoo te yéeme, ñeel jaambur ñi dul Yawut: mbóot mi moo di Almasee ngi ci yeen ñi dul Yawut itam, loolu di seen yaakaar ci ndam lu leen ñeel." 
Colossians1:28 Almasi moomu nag lanuy xamle; na mu gëna xeloo lanuy àrtoo nit ku nekk, te ni lanuy jàngale nit ku nekk, ngir àgge nit ku nekk ba fa kanam Almasi, fekk ko mat sëkk, na mu ware ku ànd ak Almasi." 
Colossians1:29 Loolu moo ma tax di góor-góorlu ci xare bii may xaree dooleem, ak manoorey jëfam, jiy liggéey ci sama jëmm jii." 
Colossians2:1 Bëgg naa nag, ngeen xam xare bu metti, bi ma leen di xareel, yeen ak waa Lawdise ak mboolem gëmkat ñi ma masula teg bët," 
Colossians2:2 ngir ngeen gëna am fit, mànkoo ci biir cofeel, te géeju ci gis-gisu xol bu leer nàññ te wóor, ba mana daj dëgg, mbóotum Yàlla, miy Almasi ci boppam." 
Colossians2:3 Ci moom la mboolem alal ji ci xel ak xam-xam, dëxëñe." 
Colossians2:4 Loolu laa leen di wax, ngir kenn bañ leena réerale ay kàdduy naxe yu mbubboo ag dëgg." 
Colossians2:5 Ndax jëmm ji kat teewul, waaye xol baa ngeek yeen, di bégee gis seen doxalin wu jekk, ak seen ngëm gu wér gu ngeen gëm Almasi." 
Colossians2:6 Kon nag, ni ngeen nangoo Almasi Yeesu di Sang bi, àndleen ak moom, jëfe noonu." 
Colossians2:7 Sampleen seeni reen ci moom, tabaxuleen ci moom, feddlikuleen ci wàllu ngëm, ni ñu leen ko jàngale, ba seenub xol baawaanal kàdduy cant." 
Colossians2:8 Moytuleen ba kenn bañ leena këfe kàdduy naxi neen yu ñu jàppe xam-xam bu xelu, kàddu yu sukkandikoowul Almasi, xanaa aaday nit, ak cëslaayi àddina." 
Colossians2:9 Ndax kat ci Almasi, ci yaramu nitam la léppi Yàlla dëkke, ba mat sëkk ci moom," 
Colossians2:10 ci moom ngeen mate it, te mooy kilifay mboolem boroom nguur yi, ak mboolem boroom sañ-sañ yi." 
Colossians2:11 Ci moom ngeen xarafe xaraf gu loxol nit deful, ndax noonu kuy xarfal nit ki di doge as lëf ci yaramu nit ki, ni la Almasi di doge ba mu set, buumu njaam gi leen dooley bàkkaar tënke woon. Noonu la Almasi di xarfalee." 
Colossians2:12 Ni ñu leen booleek moom suul, keroog ba ñu leen sóobee cim ndox, noonu ngeen dekkeendoo ak moom, ndax yeena wóolu dooley Yàlla mi ko dekkal." 
Colossians2:13 Yeen ñi doonoon ndee fa kanam Yàlla ndax seeni moy, ak seen ñàkka xaraf, ndax li ngeen dul Yawut, Yàllaa leen booleek Almasi dundalaat leen. Moo nu baal sunu moy yépp." 
Colossians2:14 Kayitu bor bi nu tiiñaloon, te dogali yoon toppe nu ko, moom moo far mbind ma, yóbbu kayit ga, daajaale ko ak Almasi ca bant ba." 
Colossians2:15 Moo dog sidditi boroom nguur yeek boroom sañ-sañ yi ci jaww ji, ñu doon ay jaam yu mu jàppe xare. Moo leen weer it ci kanam ñépp, diriwaale leen ca biir njaab ma topp ca ndam, la Almasi ame ca bant ba." 
Colossians2:16 Kon nag bu leen kenn sikkal ci ñam wu ngeen lekk, mbaa lu ngeen naan, mbaa màggal bés bu rafet, mbaa Terutel weer, ak bésub Noflaay." 
Colossians2:17 Loolu lépp takkndeeru yaram wuy jëmmal lu dikkagul, moom rekk la woon. Waaye yaram wi dëgg moo di Almasi." 
Colossians2:18 Buleen nangu kenn ku leen sikkal, te di kuy teg boppam jëfi toroxlu, di jaamu ay malaaka, topp seen gis-gisi peeñuy bopp. Ñu ni mel ñooy réy-réyloo xalaati neen yu ñu fente seen yég-yégi bakkan." 
Colossians2:19 Ñooñu jokkuwuñu ci Almasi, miy bopp bi, te ci bopp bi la yaram wi wépp di jëfandikoo siddit yeek tenqo yi, ba suuxatu, ngir lépp mànkoo ba mana màgg, ni ko Yàlla di màggale." 
Colossians2:20 Ndegam nag yeena bokk ak Almasi dee, ba teqlikoo ak li àddina def cëslaay, ana lu tax ngeen mel ni ñu bokk ci àddina ba tey, di tegoo ay dogali yoon yu mel nii:" 
Colossians2:21 «Bul jël lii, bul ñam lee, bul laal la ca des.»" 
Colossians2:22 Te mboolem yëf yooyu dogali yoon yi jëm day jeex doŋŋ bu ñu leen jëfandikoo. Loolu ay santaane aki àlluway nit doŋŋ la. 
Colossians2:23 Dëgg la, xel man naa nangu dogali yoon yu ni mel, ndax laaj na nit ki pastéefu ci diine ju mu tegool boppam, laaj na it toroxlu, ak coonoy yaram yu tukkee ci yar bu metti bu nit kiy tegoo, waaye jariñul dara ku bëgga moom bakkanam." 
Colossians3:1 Gannaaw nag yeena dekkeendoo ak Almasi, sàkkuleen la fa kaw, fa Almasi tooge ca ndijooru Yàlla." 
Colossians3:2 La fa kaw, xintewooleen ko, te ngeen ba li fi suuf," 
Colossians3:3 ndaxte dee ngeen, ba seenug dund ànd ak Almasi, làqe fa Yàlla." 
Colossians3:4 Seenug dund dëgg Almasi la, te keroog bu Almasi feeñee, yeen itam ay ànd ak moom feeñ, ba séddu ci ndamam." 
Colossians3:5 Kon nag reyleen seen cér yi bokk fii ci kaw suuf; lu mel ni powum séy, ak jëfi sobe, ak ñàkk sago ci lu jekkadi, ak xemmemtéef yu bon, ak bëgge, te loolooy bokkaale ba tey," 
Colossians3:6 yooyooy wàcce sànjum Yàlla ci kaw ñi déggadi. 
Colossians3:7 Yeen itam noonu ngeen daan jëfe bu jëkk, ba seenug dund bokkee fii ci kaw suuf." 
Colossians3:8 Waaye léegi lii lépp baleen ko: tàng xol, ak mer mu ëpp, ak coxor, ak saaga, ak waxi ñàkk kersa." 
Colossians3:9 Buleen di fenante, gannaaw seen jëmm ja woon démb, boole ngeen kook jëfinam ja mu àndal, summi," 
Colossians3:10 ba sol seen jëmm ju yees, jiy gën di yeeslu, te di gëna niru ki leen ko sàkkal, ba kera ngeen xamee, xam-xam bu mat sëkk." 
Colossians3:11 Dundin wu yees woowu amul jaambur akub Yawut, amul ku xaraf ak ku xaraful, amul ab doxandéem ak ku xayadi, amul ab jaam ak as gor, waaye Almasi mooy lépp te moo nekk ci ñépp." 
Colossians3:12 Yeenay ñi Yàlla taamu, sellal leen, sopp leen. Kon nag solooleen xolu yërmande, akug mbaax, ak woyoflu, ak jikko ju lewet, ak xolu muñ." 
Colossians3:13 Muñalanteleen te di balante, ndegam kenn a am lenn lu mu sikke moroomam. Ni leen Boroom bi baale, deeleen balantee noonu." 
Colossians3:14 Ci kaw loolu lépp nag, tegooleen cofeel; mooy xànc gi leen faste, ba seenug bennoo mat sëkk." 
Colossians3:15 Na jàmmu Almasi saytu seen xol. Ci jooju jàmm lañu leen woo, fekk leen ngeen di wenn yaram doŋŋ, te it saxooleen cant." 
Colossians3:16 Na leen kàddug Almasi dëkke, bay baawaan, ngeen di jariñoo xel mu mat sëkk mu ngeen di jànglantee, ak a artoonte. Woyeleen xolub cant, ñeel Yàlla, ay taalifi Sabóor, ak woyi tagg Yàlla, ak woy yu fentoo ci Noo gi." 
Colossians3:17 Lu ngeen mana def, muy ci wax, di ci jëf, defleen ko ci turu Sang Yeesu, tey sant Yàlla Baay bi ci moom." 
Colossians3:18 Jigéen ñi, nangul-leen seen jëkkër, noonu mu jekke ci ku bokk ci Boroom bi." 
Colossians3:19 Góor ñi, soppleen seen jabar, te buleen leen soxore." 
Colossians3:20 Xale yi, déggal-leen seeni waajur ci lépp, nde loolu mooy li Boroom bi rafetlu." 
Colossians3:21 Yeen ñiy baay, buleen yékkati seen xolu doom, ngir baña jeexal seen xol." 
Colossians3:22 Jaam yi, nangul-leen ci lépp seen sang yi ci àddina. Buleen ko defe ngistal, mbaa ngeen di ko sàkkoo lu leen neex, waaye defeleen ko yéeney xol bu dëggu, ndax ragal Boroom bi." 
Colossians3:23 Lu ngeen mana def, liggéeyeleen ko xol bu tàlli, ni bu ñeelul woon nit doŋŋ, xanaa Boroom bi." 
Colossians3:24 Te ngeen xam ne ci loxol Boroom bi ngeen di nangoo yool bi ngeen muurloo. Sang Almasi mooy ki ngeen di jaamu. 
Colossians3:25 Waaye ku def njubadi, njubadi ga mu def lay yooloo, te xejj ak seen du ci am." 
Colossians4:1 Yeen ñiy sang yi, yorleen seeni jaam, yorin wu jub te aw yoon, te ngeen xam ne yeen itam am ngeen ab Sang fa asamaan." 
Colossians4:2 Ag ñaan nag, saxooleen ko, te ngeen teewlu ci, boole ci ag cant." 
Colossians4:3 Te ngeen ñaanaale nu ci itam, ngir Yàlla ubbil nu buntu xamle kàddu gi, ngir siiwtaane mbóot mi ci Almasi, li waral ñu jéng ma." 
Colossians4:4 Ñaanleen ma man koo waxe ba mu leer nàññ ni mu ma ware. 
Colossians4:5 Jëfeleen xel mu rafet seen diggante ak aji gëmadi ñi ci biti, te jot gu ngeen am, fexeleen ba jariñoo ko." 
Colossians4:6 Na seen kàddu ànd ak yiw te am solo, te ngeen xam nu ngeen di tontoo ku nekk, tont li war." 
Colossians4:7 Mboolem lu jëm ci man nag, Tisig dina leen ko xamal. Mbokk la, soppe la, jawriñ ju wóor la, te it sama mbokkum jaam la, ci liggéeyu Boroom bi." 
Colossians4:8 Lii sax moo tax ma yónni ko ci yeen: xamal leen lu jëm ci nun, ak itam, teewaayam bu dëfal seen xol." 
Colossians4:9 Onesim lay àndal, sunu mbokk mu wóor, di sunu soppe, te mu bokk ci yeen. Ñoo leen di xamal mboolem lu fi xew." 
Colossians4:10 Aristàrk mi ma bokkal kaso bi, mu ngi leen di nuyu, moom ak Màrk rakku Barnaba. Ci mbiru Màrk moomu ngeen jotoon ndigal, ngir bu dikkee, ngeen teral ko." 
Colossians4:11 Yeesu mi ñuy wax Yustus itam, mu ngi nuyoo. Li bokk ci askanu Yawut, ñoom rekk ay liggéeyandoo ak man ngir nguurug Yàlla, te ñoo seral sama xol." 
Colossians4:12 Ab nuyoo it ñeel na leen, tukkee ci jaamub Almasi Yeesu, Epafras, mi bokk ci yeen. Ku jàmbaare ci saxoo leena ñaanal, ngir seenub taxawaay sotti te mat sëkk ci jëfe mboolem luy coobarey Yàlla." 
Colossians4:13 Maa ko seedeel ne coonoy ñaan bu réy la nekke, ngir yeen ak waa Lawdise ak waa Yerapolis." 
Colossians4:14 Ab nuyoo it ñeel na leen, tukkee ci sunu soppe, Luug, doktoor bi, ak Demas." 
Colossians4:15 Nuyul-leen nu bokk yi dëkke Lawdise, ak sunub jigéen Nimfa, ak mbooloom gëmkat, miy daje këram." 
Colossians4:16 Gannaaw bu ngeen jàngee biral, bataaxal bii ci seen biir, fexeleen it ba ñu jàng ko, biral, fa mbooloom gëmkat ma fa Lawdise, te yeen it bataaxal ba ngeen di jote Lawdise, nangeen ko jàng biral." 
Colossians4:17 Waxal-leen ma Arsipp ne ko: «Neel jàkk ci liggéey bi nga sasoo ci Boroom bi, ngir nga sottal ko.»" 
Colossians4:18 Man Póol nag maa leen bind nuyoo bii ci sama loxol bopp. Fàttlikuleen ne dañu maa tëj kaso. Yal na aw yiw ànd ak yeen! 
1Thessalonians1:1 Man la Póol, mi ànd ak Silwan ak Timote ci kàddu gii ma yékkati, ñeel mbooloom gëmkati waa Tesalonig, ñi bokk ci Yàlla Baay bi ak Sang Yeesu Almasi. Yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen." 
1Thessalonians1:2 Nu ngi sant Yàlla fu nu tollu ci yeen ñépp, te noppiwunu leena fàttliku ci sunuy ñaan," 
1Thessalonians1:3 ak di baamtu fi kanam Yàlla sunu Baay, jëf ji juddoo ci seen ngëm, ak liggéey bi sottee ci seen cofeel, ak yaakaar ji ngeen saxoo di séentu sunu Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
1Thessalonians1:4 Yeen bokki gëmkat ñi Yàlla sopp, xam nanu ne moom moo leen taamu," 
1Thessalonians1:5 ndax sunu xibaaru jàmm, bi nu leen àgge, dikkewu leen ay wax rekk, waaye manoore la leen dikkaale, ak ndimbalal Noo gu Sell gi, ak kóolute gu mat sëkk gu ngeen am. Xam ngeen moos na nu nekke woon ca seen biir, di xintewoo seen njariñ." 
1Thessalonians1:6 Aw ngeen sunuy tànk, aw it ci tànki Sang bi, nde yeena jot ci kàddu gi, ci biir njàqare ju bare, te di ko bége ci ndimbalal Noo gu Sell gi." 
1Thessalonians1:7 Moo leen taxa doon royukaay ci mboolem gëmkati diiwaani Maseduwan ak Akayi. 
1Thessalonians1:8 Ci seen biir kay la kàddug Boroom bi jollee, te yemul ci Maseduwan ak Akayi rekk, waaye seen ngëm Yàlla fépp la siiwe, ba soxlawunu cee waxati fenn dara." 
1Thessalonians1:9 Nit ñi ci seen bopp ñoo nuy waxal fépp, na sunu ngan ak yeen deme, ak ni ngeen walbatikoo ci Yàlla, dëddu tuur yi, bay jaamu Yàlla ju dëggu jiy dund," 
1Thessalonians1:10 tey séentu Doomam Yeesu mi mu dekkal, mu dikk bàyyikoo asamaan, moom mi nu jot ci sànj miy dikk." 
1Thessalonians2:1 Yeen ci seen bopp kay, bokk yi, xam ngeen ne sunu ngan ak yeen neenul." 
1Thessalonians2:2 Xam ngeen na nu jëkkoona sonne, ak na ñu nu torxale woon ca Filib, dëkk ba, bala noo dikk fa yeen. Teewul ci sunu ndimbalal Yàlla, nu ñeme leena àgge, ci biir xeex bu metti sax, xibaaru jàmm bu Yàlla bi." 
1Thessalonians2:3 Ndaxte sunub woote laloowul pexem sànke, ak mébét mu setul, akug njublaŋ." 
1Thessalonians2:4 Xanaa kay noonu nu Yàlla doyloo, ba dénk nu liggéeyu xibaaru jàmm bi, noonu lanuy waaree li neex Yàlla miy seet ab xol, te dunu ci wut bànneexu nit ñi." 
1Thessalonians2:5 Masunoo jaye, xam ngeen ko, ag bëgge it masunoo taxa jóg, Yàlla seede na ko;" 
1Thessalonians2:6 masunoo sàkku ngërëmal nit, du ci yeen, du ci ñeneen." 
1Thessalonians2:7 Manoon nanoo taafantoo li nu diy ndawi Almasi, ba diisal leen, waaye danoo lewetoon domm ci seen biir, mel ni jaboot juy topptoo ay doomam." 
1Thessalonians2:8 Noonu lanu nabe woon ci yeen, ba buggunu woona yem ci xamal leen doŋŋ xibaaru jàmm bu Yàlla, waaye danu leena sopp ba yéene woon leena jox sunu bakkan sax boole ci, ndax fi ngeen nu mujj tollu ci sunu xol." 
1Thessalonians2:9 Xanaa bokk yi, yeena ngi fàttliku sunu doñ-doñ ak sunu coono? Diir ba nu leen di yégal xibaaru jàmm bu Yàlla bi, guddi ak bëccëg lañu daan liggéeyaale, ngir baña diisal kenn ci yeen." 
1Thessalonians2:10 Yeena seede, Yàlla itam seede, sellnga ak njub, ak mucc sikk ga nu doon jëfe fa seen biir, yeen ñi gëm." 
1Thessalonians2:11 Xam ngeen ne fi baay féete doomam lanu féete kenn ku nekk ci yeen. 
1Thessalonians2:12 Ñaax nanu leen, dëfal leen, dénku leen, ngir ngeen di jëfe jëfin wu yelloo ak Yàlla, mi leen woo ci nguuram ak teraangaam." 
1Thessalonians2:13 Leneen lu nu dul noppee sante Yàlla, moo di lii: ba ngeen nangoo ci sunu làmmiñ kàddug Yàlla gi nu leen dégtal, te melul ni kàddug nit doŋŋ ngeen ko nangoo, waaye kàddug Yàlla gi mu doon ci lu wér, moom ngeen ko jële, te kàddu googu mooy liggéey ci seen biir, yeen gëmkat ñi." 
1Thessalonians2:14 Ndax kat bokk yi, yeena aw ci tànki gëmkati Almasi Yeesu ya fa mboolooy Yàlla, ya fa réewum Yuda, nde coono ya ñu daj ca Yawut ya, yeen it seeni waa réew teg nañu leen lu ni mel." 
1Thessalonians2:15 Yawut ñi ñoo rey Sang Yeesu, na ñu reye woon yonent yi, te ñoo nu bundxatal tey. Neexuñu Yàlla, te nooni ñépp lañu." 
1Thessalonians2:16 Ñoo nuy aaye nu àgge jaambur ñi dul Yawut, kàddu gi leen di musal. Noonu lañu matale seen jóorub bàkkaar yi ñu nekke naka jekk, waaye am sànj a leen mujj dab." 
1Thessalonians2:17 Nun nag bokk yi, teqale nañu nu ak yeen ab diir, waaye xol yi sorewaatoowul, xanaa jëmm yi rekk. Waaye sunu nammeel gu réy tax na noo def sunu kem kàttan, ndax yàkkamtee gise waat ak yeen." 
1Thessalonians2:18 Moo tax nu bëggoon leena seetsi, waaye Seytaane moo nu gàllankoor. Te man Póol, jéem naa leena seetsi bu dul benn yoon du ñaar." 
1Thessalonians2:19 Ndax kat, ana kan mooy sunu yaakaar, di sunu mbég, te di sunu kaala gu nuy sagooji? Xanaa du yeen, kera ca sunu kanam Boroom Yeesu, bu feeñee?" 
1Thessalonians2:20 Yeen déy, lanuy damoo, di leen bége." 
1Thessalonians3:1 Ba ñu muñee ba tële nag, ca lanu nangoo des ca Aten, nun doŋŋ." 
1Thessalonians3:2 Nu daldi yónni Timote, muy sunu mbokk, di jawriñub Yàlla bu nuy liggéeyandool ci xibaaru Almasi. Su ko defee Timote dooleel leen, feddli seen ngëm," 
1Thessalonians3:3 ngir kenn baña jàq ci biir tiis yii, ndax yeen ci seen bopp xam ngeen ne loolu lanu séddoo." 
1Thessalonians3:4 Ba nu nekkee ak yeen sax lanu leen jëkkoona wax ne dinanu daj ay coono, te xam ngeen ne noonu la ame." 
1Thessalonians3:5 Moo tax ba ma muñee ba tële, ma yónnee, ngir xam fu seen ngëm tollu, ndax ragal ne Fiirkat bi da leena fiir, ba sunuw ñaq neen." 
1Thessalonians3:6 Waaye léegi bi Timote délsee, bawoo ci yeen, xibaaru jàmm la nu àgge ci seen ngëm, ak seen cofeel, ak ni ngeen nuy bégee di fàttliku saa su nekk, te namm nu lool ni nu leen namme, nun itam." 
1Thessalonians3:7 Kon nag bokk yi, ci sunu biir mitit ak njàqare, sunu xol sedd na ci yeen ndax seen ngëm." 
1Thessalonians3:8 Léegi kay nu ngi dundaat, gannaaw yeena ngi sax ci Boroom bi." 
1Thessalonians3:9 Ndaw njukkal lu nuy dellooti Yàlla ngir yeen, ndax mboolem mbég mi nu leen di bége fi sunu kanam Yàlla!" 
1Thessalonians3:10 Guddi ak bëccëg, pastéefu xol lanuy dagaane Yàlla, ngir man leena gisaat, ba mottli li yées ci seen ngëm." 
1Thessalonians3:11 Yal na Yàlla sunu Baay ci boppam, ànd ak sunu Sang Yeesu, ngir jubal sunuw yoon ba nu agsi ci yeen." 
1Thessalonians3:12 Nii sunu cofeel ak yeen baawaane, yal na ko Boroom bi yokke ba baawaanal ag cofeel ci seen biir, ak ci seen diggante ak nit ñépp." 
1Thessalonians3:13 Yal na Boroom bi dooleele noonu seen xol, ngir kera bu sunu Sang Yeesu délsee, ànd ak ñoñam ñu sell ñépp, fekk leen sell te mucc sikk, fa kanam Yàlla sunu Baay." 
1Thessalonians4:1 Li ci des nag, bokk yi, moo di yeena nangoo ci sunu làmmiñ, jëfin wi ngeen wara jëfe ba neex Yàlla, te it moom ngeen nekke. Waaye danu leen di tinu, di leen ñaax, ci turu Sang Yeesu, ngir ngeen gënati koo jëfe." 
1Thessalonians4:2 Xam ngeen ndigal, yi nu leen jox ci turu Sang Yeesu." 
1Thessalonians4:3 Lii moo di coobarey Yàlla: ngeen sellal te mucc ci powum séy. 
1Thessalonians4:4 Su ko defee kenn ku nekk ci yeen mana moom yaramu boppam ci biir sellnga ak teddnga," 
1Thessalonians4:5 te ngeen ànd ak sago ci seeni xemmemtéef, baña mel ni niti xeet yi xamul Yàlla." 
1Thessalonians4:6 Ci moomu mbir, bu kenn ci yeen tooñ mbokkam, di aakimoo yelleefam, ndax waxoon nanu leen ko, ba artooti leen ne leen jëf ju ni mel, Boroom bee koy fey ña ko def." 
1Thessalonians4:7 Yàlla kat ci sellnga la nu woo, waaye du ci jëfin wu setul." 
1Thessalonians4:8 Kon nag ku jalax ndigal lii, du nit nga jalax, xanaa Yàlla, moom mi leen jox Noowam gu Sell." 
1Thessalonians4:9 Ci wàllu mbëggeel gi war ci biiri bokk, soxlawuleen ku leen ci bind dara, ndax yeen ci seen bopp, Yàlla tàggat na leen ci soppante," 
1Thessalonians4:10 te moom ngeen nekke seen digg ak mboolem bokki diiwaanu Maseduwan gépp. Teewul nag, bokk yi, nu di leen ñaax, ngir ngeen gënate jëfe noonu." 
1Thessalonians4:11 Sàkkuleen di jëfe jëfin wu dal, te ngeen di topptoo lu seen yoon nekk, tey dunde seenu ñaq, na nu leen ko sante woon." 
1Thessalonians4:12 Kon dingeen jekk nu ngeen di jëflantee ak ñu gëmul ña ca biti, te dungeen soxlaal kenn dara." 
1Thessalonians4:13 Bokk yi nag, buggunu ngeen réere mbirum way dawlu ñi, bay tiislu ni ñeneen ñi amul jenn yaakaar, di tiisloo." 
1Thessalonians4:14 Ndegam gëm nanu ne Yeesu dee na, ba dekki, noonu it lanu wara gëme ne Yàlla mooy dekkal way dawlu ñi gëmoon Yeesu, ba boole leen ak Yeesu, indaale." 
1Thessalonians4:15 Lii nu leen di àgge, te muy kàddug Boroom bi de, moo di nun ñi fiy dese bakkan ba kera Sang biy délsi, dunu jiitu way dawlu ñi fa moom." 
1Thessalonians4:16 Sang bi ci boppam, woote bu xumb lay wàccaalee asamaan, baatu kilifag malaaka jib, ànd ak coowal liitu Yàlla. Su ko defee ña seenug dee fekk ñu gëm Almasi ñooy jëkka dekki." 
1Thessalonians4:17 Gannaaw loolu nun ñi fi dese bakkan lees di këfandoo ak ñoom, jëme ca niir ya, ngir nu dajejeek Sang bi fa jaww ja, nu daldi nekk ak moom ba fàww." 
1Thessalonians4:18 Kon nag deeleen dëfalantee yooyu kàddu. 
1Thessalonians5:1 Waaye nag bokk yi, lu jëm ci ay àpp, ak bés ya loolu di am, soxlawuleen ku leen ci bind," 
1Thessalonians5:2 ndax yeen ci seen bopp, xam ngeen xéll ne Sang bi, ni sàccub guddi lay dikke." 
1Thessalonians5:3 Fa nit ñi naan: «Jàmm ak kaaraange dikk na,» fa la sànkute di dale ci seen kaw, ni aw mat di jekkee dal ci kaw jigéenu wérul, te kenn du ca rëcce." 
1Thessalonians5:4 Waaye yeen bokk yi, nekkuleen cig lëndëm, ba bés boobu di leen bett ni ab sàcc di bettee." 
1Thessalonians5:5 Yeen ñépp ay doomi leer ngeen, doomi bëccëg ndarakàmm; nun bokkunu dara ak guddi, mbaa ag lëndëm." 
1Thessalonians5:6 Kon nag bunu nelaw ni ñi ci des, waaye nanu teewlu, te ànd ak sunu sago." 
1Thessalonians5:7 Ndaxte ñiy nelaw, guddi lañuy nelaw; ñiy màndi it, guddi lañuy màndi." 
1Thessalonians5:8 Waaye nun ñiy waa bëccëg, nanu ànd ak sunu sago, te def ngëm ak cofeel, sunu kiiraayal dënn; yaakaaru texe di sunu mbaxanam xare." 
1Thessalonians5:9 Ndax kat Yàlla séddu nu am sànj, waaye ag mucc la nu moomale ndax sunu Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
1Thessalonians5:10 Su nuy dund, ak su nuy dee, moom moo nu deeyal, ngir nu mana ànd ak moom, dund." 
1Thessalonians5:11 Kon nag noonu ngeen di ñaaxantee, aka yokkante, nangeen ko wéye." 
1Thessalonians5:12 Gannaaw loolu bokk yi, danu leen di ñaan, ñi féetewoo coonob liggéey ci seen biir te jiite leen ci yoonu Boroom bi, di leen yee, nangeen leen yég." 
1Thessalonians5:13 Nangeen leen nawe seen kem kàttan te soppe leen noonu ndax seen liggéey. Gannaaw loolu, nangeen jàmmoo." 
1Thessalonians5:14 Bokk yi, danu leen di dénku; yaafus yi, femmuleen leen; ñi néewu fit, ñaaxleen leen; néew-doole yi, dimbalileen leen, te it muñal-leen ñépp." 
1Thessalonians5:15 Fexeleen ba kenn du feyantoo. Waaye lu baax, deeleen ko deflante ci seen biir, te di ko defal ñépp." 
1Thessalonians5:16 Fu ngeen tollu bégleen," 
1Thessalonians5:17 saxooleen ñaan," 
1Thessalonians5:18 te deeleen sant, ak nu mu mana deme, ndax loolu mooy coobarey Yàlla ci yeen ñi ànd ak Almasi Yeesu." 
1Thessalonians5:19 Buleen giimal taalub Noowug Yàlla gi," 
1Thessalonians5:20 buleen gàttañlu ay kàdduy waxyu. 
1Thessalonians5:21 Waaye lu mu mana doon, settantal-leen ko, li baax, ngeen jàpp ci," 
1Thessalonians5:22 te lu bon, ak nu mu mana bindoo, dàndleen ko." 
1Thessalonians5:23 Yàlla ci boppam, moom miy Boroom jàmm, yal na leen sellal, ba ngeen mat sëkk, te seen léppi xel, ak seen léppi xol, ak seen léppi yaram sàmmu, ba mucc sikk, ba kera bés bu sunu Sang Yeesu Almasi feeñee." 
1Thessalonians5:24 Ki leen woo de ku wóor la, te moo koy def it." 
1Thessalonians5:25 Bokk yi, nun itam, ñaanal-leen nu." 
1Thessalonians5:26 Nuyul-leen nu bokk yépp, te fóonal-leen nu leen na mu gëna selle." 
1Thessalonians5:27 Maa ngi leen di dénku nag, ngir Boroom bi, jàngleen biral bataaxal bii ngir bokk yépp." 
1Thessalonians5:28 Yal na sunu yiwu Boroom Yeesu Almasi ànd ak yeen. 
2Thessalonians1:1 Man la Póol, mi ànd ak Silwan ak Timote ci kàddu gii ma yékkati, ñeel mbooloom gëmkati waa Tesalonig, ñi bokk ci Yàlla sunu Baay, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
2Thessalonians1:2 Aw yiw ak jàmm ñeel na leen, tukkee ci Yàlla sunu Baay, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
2Thessalonians1:3 Bokk yi, manunoo ñàkka sant Yàlla ci yeen fu nu tollu, te muy lu jaadu, gannaaw seen ngëm a ngi yokku bu baaxa baax, te cofeelu ku nekk ci yeen ñépp di gënatee law, digganteem ak moroomam." 
2Thessalonians1:4 Moo tax nun, nu di leen damoo fi biir mboolooy gëmkati Yàlla yi, ndax seenug muñ, ak seen ngëm, ci biir mboolem ni ñu leen di bundxatale, ak njàqare yi ngeen di jànkoonteel." 
2Thessalonians1:5 Loolu lépp di firndeel njekku àtteb Yàlla, bi leen di yellale nguurug Yàlla, gi tax ngeen di sonn." 
2Thessalonians1:6 Te kat njekku Yàlla dina feeñ ndax coono ba muy delloo ñi leen teg ab coono. 
2Thessalonians1:7 Dina feeñ it ndax noflaay ba mu nuy booleek yeen ñiy dékku ab coono, sédde nu ko, kera bés bu Sang Yeesu feeñee, ànd ak ay malaakaam yu làmboo manooreem, wàcce asamaan." 
2Thessalonians1:8 Ci biir sawara wuy sëlsëli lay doon. Ca lay mbugal ñi xamul Yàlla, ak ñi baña déggal xibaaru jàmm bi jëm ci sunu Boroom Yeesu." 
2Thessalonians1:9 Ñooñu lees di mbugale sànkute gu sax dàkk, fu sore Boroom bi, sore teddngay manooreem," 
2Thessalonians1:10 kera bés bu délsee ba jot ci teddngaam ci biir ñoñam ñu sell ñi, ba mboolem ñi ko gëm di ko yéemoo. Te yeen ci seen bopp, ci ngeen di bokk, ndax yeena gëm la nu leen seedeeloon." 
2Thessalonians1:11 Moo tax nu saxoo leena ñaanal, ngir sunu Yàlla yellale leen ab wooteem, ngir itam mu sottale kàttanam seen mboolem mébét mu baax, ak seen jépp jëf ju laloo ngëm." 
2Thessalonians1:12 Su ko defee sunu turu Sang Yeesu màgge ci yeen, yeen it, ngeen màgge ci moom, ci sunu ndimbalal yiwu Yàlla, ak Sang Yeesu Almasi." 
2Thessalonians2:1 Léegi nag, bokk yi, ci wàllu dellusig sunu Sang Yeesu Almasi, ak sunu dajeji fa moom, li nu leen di ñaan moo di:" 
2Thessalonians2:2 bu leen lenn gaawa xañ sago ba ngeen ñàkka ànd ak seenum xel, mbaa mu di leen jaaxal; du lu ñu ne kàddug waxyu la, du genn kàddu mbaa bataaxal bu ñu nu moomale, te di leen gëmloo ne bésu Sang bi dikk na ba noppi." 
2Thessalonians2:3 Bu leen kenn naxe nenn, ndax bés ba du dikkagum, te fippu gu mag ga jëkkula dikk, ba ki jëmmal ndëngte te dëgmal alkute, feeñ." 
2Thessalonians2:4 Kooku mooy jànkoonteeka damu ci kaw mboolem lees di wooye yàlla, mbaa lees di jaamu, te mooy mujj toog ca kër Yàlla ga, ba far tudde boppam Yàlla." 
2Thessalonians2:5 Xanaa fàttlikuwuleen ne waxoon naa leen ko, ba ma nekkee ak yeen?" 
2Thessalonians2:6 Te xam ngeen li ko téye léegi, ba du mana feeñ lu dul ca bésam."
